(7) yaduktaM prAchuryeNa kR^iShNA pR^ithivIti tatra pramANamAha - rakto.agniriti || 'agniH' tejo 'rakto' raktasvarUpa ityuktam | udakaM svataH shuklam | evaM pR^ithivI 'svato' nirupAdhikatayA kR^iShNaiva | svata ityasya kR^ityaM darshayati - nAbhIti | viShNoriti sheShaH | padmasya lokAdhAratvAtpItarUpavattvAchcheti bhAvaH | padmasambandhAdityuktyA prAksthitAnAmeva lokAnAM padmadalaiH sambandho, na tu pAdmasR^iShTau prAgvilInAnAM padmadalaiH sR^iShTiriti j~nAyate | 'sA' pR^ithivI| tasyA evaupAdhikaM rUpAntaramAha - kShatreti| duShTakShatriyANAM raktAbhisambandhAt sA raktetyabhidhIyata ityarthaH | tasyA evaupAdhikaM rUpAntaramAha - udakabahutvata iti| udakasambandhabAhulyAdityarthaH| 'eti' prApnoti| setyasti | evameveti | pR^ithivyAM varNAntarasya varNavisheShasya 'evameva' vakShyamANarItyA 'gatiH' sthitirbhavedityarthaH | evamevetyuktameva darshayati - viShNviti | 'vIryAbhiyogAt' vIryasambandhAt, vIryavikArANDadvAreti bhAvaH | na kevalaM padmasambandhAt, kiM tu vIryasambandhAchcheti nimittasamuchchaye chashabdaH | vIryasambandhe.api kutaH pItvaM bhuva ityata Aha - svarNeti| hishabdo bhagavataH svarNavIryatve 'tadaNDamabhavaddhaimam' shuShmaM 'hiraNyAtmakam' ityAdipramANaprasiddhidyotakaH | svarNasya pItatvamapyanenaiva siddham | yata ityarthe vA hishabdaH | nanvanyatrAdR^iShTaM viShNuvIryasya suvarNatvaM kathaM kalpyate, vIryasambandhAtpUrvaM nimittAbhAvashchetyata Aha - anAdiH puruShottama iti | tathA cha viShNoranAditvena tadvIryasambandhasyApi pravAhato.anAditvAnna nimittAbhAvaH | laukikakSharAkSharapuruShavilakShaNatvAnna dR^iShTavirodha iti bhAvaH | parameshvara iti pAThe tu aishvaryamuktArthaghaTakatayA vyAkhyeyamiti | vyomasaMhitAyAmityasya kArShNyaprachuretyuktamityadhyAhR^itenAnvayaH | anena prachuretyuktiprayojanamuktaM bhavati || 6 ||
|| iti pR^ithivyadhikaraNam || 6 ||
|| 7. tadabhidhyAnAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe brahmaNaH prakR^itAdhibhUtAdhidaivaviShayasaMhR^itikartR^itve shrutivirodhaH parihriyate | pUrvapakShayati - prANAnAmiti || taittirIyashrutiriyam | AdishabdAdevaMvidhashrutyantarANi pAtR^itvAditi yuktishcha gR^ihyate | vyAkhyAteyaM shrutirdyubhvAdhikaraNe | 'anyo' viShNoH rudra evetyarthaH ||
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || itItyanantaraM shrutAviti sheShaH | bandhalayasyetyanena tadityasyAvR^ittirdarshitA | anAderityAdau grAhyam | asya tatkartR^itvamityanenAnvayaH | atra tatkartR^ikatvaM tadichChAdhInatvaM vivakShitam| tataH kimityatastalliN^gAdityasya tachcha tat liN^gaM cheti vigrahAshrayeNArthamAha - tadabhidhyAneti | bandhalayasyetyatrApyanvIyate | tathA cha bandhasya saMsArasya layasya tasmAnmokShasyeshvarechChAdhInatvarUpahetorityarthaH | shrutAdityadhyAhAre liN^gAdityasyeti shrutAlliN^gAttatkartR^itvaM pratIyata ityanvayaH | atra tatkartR^ikatvaM tatkR^ityadhInatvaM, pratIyata ityasya chAnumIyata ityarthaH | bandhalayasyechChAdhInatvali
N^gena tatprayatnAdhInatvAnumAnopapatteriti bhAvaH | tataH kimityato.anAdibandhalayakartR^itveneshvarasya sAdijagatsaMhR^itikartR^itvaM paratayA vyAkhyAti - kimviti | layasya tatkartR^itvamityamuShajyate | sidhyatIti sheShaH | nanvastu viShNoranAdibhavabhetturvishvasaMhArakartR^itvaM, tAvatA prayatnAkhyatatsaMhAraphalopadhAnaM kutaH sidhyatItyata Aha - ityetasmAditi | ityetadrUpAt sAdijagatsaMhartR^itvarUpAddhetorevetyarthaH | sUtre uddeshyasamarpakapadAbhAvAdyogyatayA labdhaM taddarshayati - sarveti | vidheyasamarpakasya sa ityasyArtho viShNuriti | nikhilanigamatAtparyaprasAdhitajagatkartR^itvAdinA tasyaiva prastutatvAditi bhAvaH | yadvA - sa ityasyAvR^ittyoddeshyavidheyaparatvamityAshayena sarvasaMhArakartA viShNuriti choktam | viShNuriti sAvadhAraNam | ata eva sUtre.avadhAraNArthakastushabdaH prAyoji | nanvastvIshvarechChAdhInatvamanAdibandhalayasyeshvarakartR^ikatve liN^gam, astu chAnAdibandhalayasyeshvarakartR^ikatvaM sAdijagatsaMhartR^itve | tathApi sAdijagallayakartR^itvaM tatsaMhartR^itvaM kathaM liN^gamubhayorabhedAditi chenna | saMhArakartR^itvashakterhetutvena tatkartR^itvaphalopadhAnasya sAdhyatvenAbhyupagamena abhedAbhAvAt ||
(3) sautramevashabdaM kaimutyAntaraparatayA vyAkhyAti - kimviti || idaM chAvartate | kimvityAdishrutibhya ityanvayaH | tathA cha yadA liN^gAdeva siddhyati, tadA kimu shrutyA balavatyA sidhyatIti | yadaikayaiva spaShTashrutyA viShNureva saMhArakartR^itvena siddhyati, tadA kimu vaktavyaM bahushrutibhya ityarthaH| ityevashabda iti | sUchayatIti sheShaH | tathA cha ityevamarthaM sautra evashabdo j~nApayatItyarthaH | anena sUtre tadabhidhyAnAditishrutiyuktisUchake vyadhikaraNae paJNchamyAviti sUchitam | tathA chAyaM sUtrArthaH - 'tadabhidhyAnAt' 'tasyAbhilliN^gAt' iti shrutau tadabhidhyAnahetukatvashravaNAt, 'talliN^gAt' tasmAlliN^gAt sAdijagallayakartR^itvamIshvarasya sutarAM sidhyati | tatashcha 'talliN^gAt' sAdijagatsaMhR^itishaktatvarUpAlliN^gAt sa tu viShNureva sarvasaMhArakartA siddhaH | yadA sAdijagatsaMharaNasAmarthyarUpaliN^gAdeveshvaraH sarvasaMhartAsidhyati, tadA sutarAM 'yamapyeti' iti spaShTashrutyA yadaikayaiva sidhyati kimu tadA bahushrutibhya iti | chandrikAyAM tu tushabdo.abhidhyAnagatasya saMjihIrShAtvarUpavisheShasya dyotakaH | samAnAdhikaraNe paJNchamyau | tathA cha tasyAbhidhyAnAditi shrutyuktAddhareranAdibandhasaJNjihIrShArUpAt 'talliN^gAt' sAdijagatsaMhartR^itvaliN^gAt yo.anAdisraShTR^itvena prakR^ito yashcha janakatvena mArakatayA shaktito yashcha 'oM tatsaditi nirdeshaH' iti smR^itisiddhaH tachChabdavAchyatvenoktaH 'sa no hariH' iti shrutau cha sa ityuktaH, sa eva hariH saMharteti sUtrayojanAM pradarshya TIkA.apyetatparetyuktam | shrutau bhUyashcheta chashabdo vIpsAyAm | jAtAditi sheShaH | tathA cha tasmin bhagavati tasya manasaH saMyojanAdbhUyo bhUyaH 'tattvabhAvAt' punaH punastasya bhagavato yathArthadhyAnAdyAthArthyaj~nAnAchcha jAtAt 'abhidhyAnAchcha' madhyamaprasAdarUpAdbhagavadichChAvisheShAt 'ante' paripAkakAle prArabdhakarmAvasAne sati vishvabandhakamAyAnivR^ittirbhavati ityarthaH | ata eva tR^itIyAdhyAye avyaktAdhikaraNe tasyAbhidhyAnAdichChayA prasAdena saMsAro nivartate ityuchyate | etachcha mokShasya prasAdasAdhyatve liN^gaM bhagavatprasAdena taddarshanabhAvaM cha j~nApayati - dR^iShTvaiva taM muchyata iti | mokShasya darshanasAdhyatvashravaNAtprasAdAddarshanaM darshanAnmokSha ityavashyamaN^gIkAryatvAditi TIkAvachanamuktArthAnukUlam | paripAkakAla ityetadadhikaraNIyaTIkApadasyopAsanAjanitaprasAdAddarshane jAte sati prArabdhakarmAvasAne satIti chArthaH | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - tasya viShNorabhidhyAnAdvishvamAyAnivR^ittiH kutaH jAtA | tasminneva manoyojanAdbhayobhUyastattvabhAvanayA chAnte.aparokShaj~nAne jAte vishvabandhakamAyAni
vR^ittidvArako mokSho bhavatIti | uktaM cha sudhAyAm - asyAparokShaj~nAne jAte ante karmakShayAnta iti | atra mAyAshabdena mAyAà¤¼.avidyAprakR^itirityAdishabdAbhidhyamanAdyeva kimapi dravyamaN^gIkaraNIyamiti sudhokteH,
aje dve prakR^itI duShTe nR^iShu prAtisvikaM sthite |
svagaNAchChAdikA tvekA paramAchChAdikA parA ||
svaguNAchChAdikAM hatvA paramAchchAdikAM paraH |
vyAghuTya mokShapadavIM dadAta puruShottamaH ||
iti smR^itisiddhe dvirUpe duShTaprakR^itI gR^ihyete | tayorduShTatvaM cha sa eveshvaraH svaprakAshamapi svarUpachaitanyaM svAdhiShThAnalabdhapariNAmamahadahaN^kArAdiprakR^ityaMshaiH saMyojyAvidyamAnamevAsya kartR^itvAdi svAtantryAdi pradarshya rAgAdyutpAdanadvArA duHkhamanubhAvayatIti sudhoktarItyA jIvasya duShTatvasampAdakatvAt, 'ajAmajitadoShagR^ihItaguNAn' (bhAga.10. 14.15.) iti vachanAchcha siddham | jaDaprakR^iterbandhakatvaM chitprakR^itidvArA, chitprakR^iterbandhakatvaM tu 'daivI hyeShA guNamayI mama mAyA duratyayA' iti smR^itisiddham | eShA tu asya mohikA iti vyAkhyAnAt anyaprakR^itidvayamapyasti, tachcha 'athAnye prakR^itI duShTe' ityAdivachanAtsiddhaM, duShTatvamapi ata eva tayoH siddhyati | anAdiprakR^iteH kIdR^isho vinAsha iti chetsudhoktarItyA svarUpapradhvaMsa eveti gR^ihANa | na cha duShTaprakR^ityorubhayoH svarUpeNa nivR^ittyabhyupagame shrutigItAtAtparyodAhR^itashrutau hana drAvayetyuktivirodhaH, smR^itAvapi vyAghuTyetyuktivirodhashcheti vAchyam | vyAghuTyetyasya nihatyetyarthAbhyupagamAt| prathamaM drAvaya pashchAddhanetyarthasambhavAchcha | shrutau vishvashabdaH ekaikAsheShaparaH na tu samastAsheShaparaH | ekaikasya prAtisvikamAyAnivR^ittAvapi sarvamAyAnivR^itterabhAvAt | ata eva R^igbhAShye prAtisvikI prakR^itiryattamashcha doShAshchAnye puMsyato yuktametadityuktam| sudhAyAM cha ekamuktau na sarvamuktiH, pratijIvamavidyAbhedAN^gIkArAdityuktam | idaM tvavadheyam - jIvasya na mAyaivAvaraNaM kintvanyAnyapyAvaraNAni santi | tAni chAdau dehaH tataH prakR^itibandhaH tataH sattvAdiguNabandhaH tataH karmAdibandhaH tataH liN^gadehaH tataH IshvarechChetyevaMrUpANi | na chAtra mUlAbhAvaH | dehAdbAhyaM vinA.atIvabAhyatvAditi gItAbhAShyasya mUlatvAt | idaM hi bhAShyaM prameyadIpe dehAdbAhyaM vinA.a.atmAbhimAnasthamadhyAtmam, tatra yuktiH - atIvabAhyatvAdatyabhimAnaviShayatvAbhAvAditi vyAkhyAtam | atra dehAdbAhyasya gehAderadhyAtmatvAbhAve sAdhye jIvApekShayA.atIvabAhyatvAditi heturuktaH | asya hetorvyabhichAravAraNAyAtyabhimAnaviShayatvAbhAvAditi vyAkhyAtaH | tathA cha jIvApekShayA dehasyAtIvabAhyatvAt madhye bahUnyAvaraNAni santIti siddhamiti | na chAparokShaj~nAne jAte satItyarthAbhyupagame tannirdhAraNAdhikaraNavirodhaH, tatra shravaNAderevAj~nAnanivartakatvokteH | atrApi punaH punarbhagavati mano
yojanatattvabhAvajanitAbhidhyAnasya shravaNAdijanitaprasAdarUpasya mAyAnivartakatvokteshcheti vAchyam | yato.aj~nAnasya shravaNAdinivartyatve.apyaparokShaj~nAnanivartyatvamapi sambhavati | shravaNajanitaparokShaj~nAnena aj~nAnasya shithilIbhAvarUpanivR^ittiH aparokShaj~nAnenAtyantikI nivR^ittirityabhyupagamAt | etatsarvaM
j~nAnena tu tadaj~nAnaM yeShAM nAshitamAtmanaH |
teShAmAdityavajj~nAnaM prakAshayati tatparam ||
iti gItAbhAShyaprameyadIpikayoH spaShTamapavarNitam | tathA hi prameyadIpavachanaM svarUpaj~nAnamavidyayA.a.avR^itaM, vR^ittij~nAnaM tvavidyAM shithilayati| brahma prakAshayatIti| atra vR^ittij~nAnashabdasya gItAbhAShyarItyA parokShamaparokShaM chArthaH| na chaivaM pramANairutpannamapIdaM manovR^ittirUpatattvaj~nAnam antaraN^gabhUtena vishuddhasvabhAvarUpaj~nAnenopodbalitaM sat bahiraN^gamanAdyapi savAsanamevAj~nAnaM samUlaghAtaM hantIti sudhAvirodhaH | atra kevalavR^ittij~nAnasyAj~nAnanivartakatvokteraj~nAnanivartane svarUpaj~nAnasyApi vR^ittij~nAnasahAyatvokteshcheti vAchyam | pUrvaM svarUpaj~nAnasyAvR^itatvenAkiJNchitkaratve.api parokShavR^ittij~nAnenAvarakAj~nAnasya shithilIbhAvAnantaramaparokShavR^ittij~nAnopodbalakatvasambhavAtkevalasyAparokShavR^ittirj~nAnasyAtyantikAj~nAnanivartakatvAbhAve.api svarUpaj~nAnopodbalitasya samUlAj~nAnaghAtakatvopapatteshcha | yamapyetIti shrutirattAdhikaraNe vyAkhyAtA | ya idamityanyashrutyarthastu | yasmAdyaH 'idaM sarvaM' vishvaM 'vilApayati' nAshayati tasmAtsa bhagavAn saMhartR^itvAddharirityuchyate | na cha pitR^itvAnnAshakatvAyogaH | yataH sa 'paro' mamatvAdidoSharAhityAllokapitR^ivilakShaNaH | tatkatham? yataH sa paramAtmA sarvotkR^iShTachetano.ata iti |
(4) viShNoreva saMhartR^itve 'rudro mA.a.avishAntakaH' (mahA.16.2.) ityukta shrutivirodha ityata Aha-sraShTeti|| yato hariH parameshvaro Ishebhyo brahmAdibhyo vara uttamo.atra eka eva sraShTA 'pAtA' rakShitA saMhartA cha bhavati | tato.anyeShAM brahmAdInAM sraShTR^itvAdikaM 'dAruyoShAvat' dArumayastrIpratimAvat paratantramuchyate purANAdAvityarthaH | tadapi na sAmastyenetyAha - ekadesha iti | sR^iShTyAdikamiti pUrvatrApi sambadhyate 
| cho.avadhAraNe.apyarthe cha | tathA chAtra paratantre.apyanyaniShThasraShTR^itvAdAvekadeshasya kriyaiva jagadekadeshaviShayaiva sR^iShTyAdikriyA niviShTA, na tu 'sarvAtmanA' sarvathA sarvajagatsambandhisR^iShTyAdikamIritaM niviShTamuktamityarthaH | yadvA - paratantre.api brahmAdijIve 'ekadeshakriyA' jagadekadeshasyaiva kriyA sR^iShTyAdirUpA tatkartR^itvamiti yAvat | 'na tu sarvAtmanA' sarvathA sarvajagatsambandhisR^iShTyAdikaM tatkartR^itvamIritaM pramANeShu | tarhi samastaM sR^iShTyAdikaM kasmAdbhavedityata Aha - sR^iShTyAdikamiti | tushabdo visheShArthaH | parAditi hetugarbham | tathA cha 'samastaM' sarvajagatsambandhisR^iShTyAdikaM 'parAt' svatantrAdviShNoreva bhavet, na tvanyasmAdityarthaH | tathA chAntakatvashrutiH parAdhInasaMhArakartR^itvaparA paratantrajagadekadeshasaMhR^itikartR^itvaviShayatayA bhAktA cheti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH | skAnda ityanantaramuktamiti sheShaH |
(5) rudrasya saMhAre pAratantryaM cha viShNukartR^ike tasmin dvAratvameveti bhAvenAha - nimittamiti || dashamaskandhe uddhavavAkyametat | taveti kR^iShNa uchyate | tasya kAlAkhyarUpANi iti hetugarbhaM visheShaNam | AkhyA cha rUpaM  AkhyArUpe kAla ityAkhyArUpe yasyAsau kAlAkhyArUpI tasyeti vigrahaH | yasyeti bahuvrIhij~nApakaTIkA tu inerarthakathanaparA | rUpasyAkR^iteH kAlatvaM sarvasaMhartR^itvAdiguNasampannatvaM, kAlashabdo jagadbandhanachChedanaj~nAnAdisarvabhagavaddharmavAchIti gItAbhAShyokteH | dharmavishiShTabhagavadvAchIti tadarthaH | yadvA - 'viShNau chAdhIshvare chittaM dhArayan kAlavigrahaH' iti gItAbhAShyodAhR^itasmR^iteH prameyadIpe kAlanAmA vigraho yasyAsau tathokta iti vyAkhyAnAdatrApi saptamyantarUpapadaghaTitabahuvrIhisamAsavigrahapradarshakatayA TIkA vyAkhyeyA | na chaivaM kAlAkhyArUpiNa iti na syAditi vAchyam | ArUpiNo vyAptarUpiNa iti AN^ prashleShAt | asya kAla ityAkhyayA yuktaM rUpamasyAstIti madhyamapadalopitvAdvA | tattvapradIpe tu - kAlAkhyaiva kAla iti nAmaiva rUpaM j~nApakaM vAchakatvena tadvAniti vyAkhyAtam | tathA cha kAlAkhyArUpiNa Ishasya tava 'vishvasarganirodhayoH' jagatsR^iShTisaMhArayoH hiraNyagarbhaH sharvashcha 'nimittamAtraM' dvAramAtraM na tu svatantrakAraNamityarthaH | iti cheti chashabdo na kevalaM skAnde, kintu bhAgavate cheti samuchchayArthaH atrApi pUrvavadeva sheShaH |
(6) bhAgavatasmR^itermUlabhUtAM shrutiM chAha - sa iti || sa viShNuH brahmaNA dvArabhUteneti sheShaH | evaM rudreNetyatrApi | 'visR^ijati' vividhaM sR^ijati | 'vilApayati' vinAshayati | sR^iShTyAdau viShNoreva mukhyakAraNatve hetumAha - so.anutpattiralayo yata iti | utpattinAshashUnya ityarthaH | sa eka eva harirityanvayaH | 'paraH' uttamo vilakShaNo vA | anena mamatvAdidoSharAhityena lokapitR^ivailakShaNyAlloke pituranyasya mArakatve.api prakR^ite pitureva viShNormArakatvoktau na lokavirodhaH, tasyAdoShatvAditi sUchitam | 'parAnandaH' 
pUrNAnandaH nirduHkhatvaM choktam | mahopaniShadItyasya brahmarudrayordvAratvamevoktamityadhyAhAreNAnvayaH |  
|| iti tadabhidhyAnAdhikaraNam || 7 ||
|| 8. viparyayAdhikaraNam ||
(1) asminnadhikaraNe adhibhUtAdisaMhArakramaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate | atra prakR^itAdhibhUtAdIni kimutpattikramAnusAreNa bhagavatA lIyante vyutkrameNa veti sandehasya bIjabhUtaM shrutivigAnaM darshayati - ata eveti || pUrvaprakR^itAdeva 'parAt' uttamAt 'idaM' jagat 'kramAt' tattvadevatAtAratamyakrameNaivotpadyate, krameNaiva lIyata ityarthaH | na jagadvatparamAtmA.apyutpattinAshavAnityAha - neti | 'asau' paramAtmA 'nodeti' notpadyate 'astaM' nAshaM 'naiti' na prApnotItyarthaH | shrItattvavyAvR^ityarthaM paramAdakSharAdviShNoriti | na tvanyasmAditi prathamaivakArasya vyutkramAdeveti dvitIyasya na tvanyasminniti tR^itIyasya chArthaH | utpattikrameNaiva lIyante 'ata eva' iti shruterlokAnukUlyAchcha |
(2) iti prApte siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || kramavachanamapItyanena sUtre AvR^ittaH kramashabdaH kramavachanaparaH | apyarthasturityuktaM bhavati | apiH bAdhakatvena upanyastamapIti visheShaNasamuchchayArthaH | AvR^ittasya viparyayeNetyasyArthaH viparIteti | pravR^ittaM yata iti sheShaH | asyAto layakramaH viparyayeNa utpattikramavaiparItyenaiveti sautrapadoktasAdhyenAnvayaH ||
(3) kutaH kramashruterarthAntarakalpanamityato.api pravR^ittam ata iti padaM tushabdArthAvadhAraNAnvitatayA.anUdya vyAkhyAti - karteti || kartetyataH prAk ata evetyuttaravachanAt kuta ityupaskAryam | yasyAmeva shrutau kramAllayaH shrUyate, tasyAmeva vachanAt na tvanyasyAmityevashabdArthaH | yaH 'prANAdikasya' brahmAdikasyAsya jagataH kramAtkartA yashcha 'bhUmyAdikasyAsya' vyutkramAddhantA sa harireva paro, na tvanya ityarthaH | anenotpattAvuttamakramaH, laye tvadhamakrama iti sUchitam ||
(4) nanu shrutitvAvisheShAt vyutkramashrutyA kramashruteH kuto bAdhaH, viparItameva kiM na syAdityato.ataHshabdasUchitAM smR^itimAha - anurUpa iti || yojanA tu - kramo dvividhaH anurUpaH pratirUpashcheti | tatra 
sR^iShTau yaH kramaH so.anurUpaH | uttamAditAratamyAnusAritvAt | yo laye kramaH sa pratirUpaH uttamAditAratamyapratikUlatvAt | evamubhayavidhakrameNa 'vibhuH' samartho bhagavAn sR^iShTisaMhArakarteti | pAdma ityanantaraM vachanAdityanuShajyate | asya sAvakAshakramashruterniravakAshavyutkramapadaghaTitashrutyA bAdho yukta ityadhyAhR^itasAdhyavAkyenAnvayaH || 
(5) vyutkramAllayAN^gIkAre lokavirodhApAtAnnAsau yuktaH, loke prAyeNa pUrvotpannAnAM pitrAdInAM prathamaM layadarshanAdityataH pravR^ittamataH shabdAvR^ittyA upapadyate chetyaMshaM vyAchaShTe - pUrvotpannAnAmityarthaH | upapadyata ityataH prAk laye kramo viparyayeNeti sUtrAMsha AvR^ittyA saMyojyaH | upapadyata ityasya sAmarthyAdhikyayuktyA siddhyatItyarthaH | yadvA - upapadyata ityasya yujyata ityarthaH | sAmarthyAdhikyaM tvatashshabdArthaH | na kevalaM shrUyate, kintu yujyate cheti samuchchaye chashabdaH | tathA cha laukikAnAM prAyashshatavarShajIvitvAdirUpasya balaj~nAnAdirUpasya vA sAmarthyasya sAmyAt kramAllaye.api nAsAvalaukikatattvadevatAlaye bhavati, yataH pUrvotpannAnAM sAmarthyAdhikyAduttareShAM tadabhAvAt, evaJNcha laukikavirodhasyaiva guNatvAditi bhAvaH | pUrvotpanneShu sarvatra uttarotpannApekShayA sAmarthyAdhikyamastIti j~nApanAya dvirvachanam | anena - yataH 'kramastu' kramavachanamapi 'viparyayeNa' viparItakramApekShayA pravR^ittamato laye kramaH 'viparyayeNa tu' utpattikramavaiparItyenaiva | kuto.arthAkramashruteH kuto bAdhaH shrutitvAvisheShAt viparItaM kiM na syAt | ata eva sAvakAshatvAdeva | na cha lokavirodhaH | yata upapadyate chAyaM vyatkramo yujyate cha | katham? ataH sAmarthyAdhikyAt | na kevalaM shrutyochyate vyutkramaH kintu upapadyate cheti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati ||
(6) nanu pUrvotpannAnAM sAmarthyAdhikyameva kutaH? yena pashchAllayaH syAdityata Aha - vAmane cheti || sAmatsyaM vIpsArthaH | tathA cha yataH 'pUrve pUrve' AdisR^iShTau pUrvotpanneShu chaturmukhAditattvadeveShu viShNoH 'sannidhAnaM' sannidhiH 'kramAdhikaM' tAratamyakrameNAdhikam ata eva teShAM pUrvotpannAnAM pashchAdutpannApekShayA 'sAmarthyAdhikyam' balaj~nAnashaktyAdhikyamevAsti | na kevalametAvat, kintu teShAM 'vyAptiH' aNDAdbahiH svasvAbhimanyamAnaparyantaM dehato vyAptirapi tAratamyakrameNAdhikaiva, na nyUnA samA cha | yata evam atasteShAM pashchAdeva layo na kadAchitpUrvaM, nAtra saMshaya ityarthaH | tathAshabda upamAyAM samuchchaye vA | tena pashchAdutpanneShu uktavaiparItyaM cha sidhyati | 'pUrvAdibhyo navabhyo vA' iti sarvanAmasaMj~nAyAM vikalpAnushAsanAt tadabhAvapakShe pUrve ityetatsaptamyantaM, tadbhAvapakShe tu prathamAbahuvachanamidam | na cha tathAtve sannidhAnamityasyAnanvayaH sannidhIyate viShNuratreti vyutpattyA.asya pratimAparatvAt | tathAtve 'pUrve pUrve' pUrvapUrvamutpannAstattavadevAH yato viShNoH 'kramAdhikaM sannidhAnaM' krameNAdhikapratimArUpA iti yojanA | iti vAmana ityanvayaH 
| vachanAdityatrApyanuShajyate | na sAmarthyAdhikyAsiddhirityadyAhR^itenAnvayaH |
|| iti  viparyayAdhikaraNam || 8 ||
|| 9. antarAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe pUrvoktavyutkrameNa laye vij~nAnAdau kvachidapavAdashaN^kA nirAkriyate | pUrvapakShasya sUtra evoktatvAt tatpaThitvA pUrvapakShAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - antareti || talliN^gAdityetachChrutyuktAtkramAdutpattikramAllayAkhyaliN^gAdityarthaH | yadvA - ityetadrUpAlliN^gadarshanAdityarthaH | manasaH pUrvotpannatve 'prANAnmanaH' iti shrutyudAharaNena tasya pUrvameva laye 'yachChet' iti shratyudAharaNena chobhayorasiddhiH parihR^itA | pUrvapakShe prANAt 'mano' manastattvaM jAtaM tato vij~nAnatattvaM jAtamityarthaH | siddhAnte tu - mukhyaprANAnmanorUpendriyaM, tasmAdvR^ittirUpaM vij~nAnam utpannamityarthaH | yachChediti kAThakavAkye pUrvapakShe manashshabdastattvaparaH siddhAnte.arthastu - 'prAj~no' j~nAnI 'vAk' vAktatvaM tadabhimAninI umA 'manasI' manastattve tadabhimAnini rudre 'yachChet' uparamettadvashatvAttatra lIyata iti smarediti yAvat | 'tat' manaH 'j~nAna Atmani' vij~nAnatattvAbhimAninyAM vANyAM lIyata iti dhyAyediti | prameyadIpe tu - 'yachChet' niyachChediti kAThakabhAShyAnurodhAt 'vAk' vAchaM manasi 'yachChet' tanniyatAM dhyAyet vAgadevatAM manodevatAdhInatayA chintayediti vipariNAmAshrayeNa adhyAhAraM layaparatvaM cha vinA vyAkhyAtam | ata eva tattvapradIpakAro.api vAchaM manasi yachChet ityevAha | manasIti dIrghashChAndasaH | vAN^manasI parasparaM 'yachChet' ekaikatraikaikaM yachChet iti vyAkhyAnaM tUdAhR^itagranthaviruddham | hetvaMshaM vyAkhyAya pUrvapakShapratij~nAMshaM vyAchaShTe - vij~nAnamasanI iti | tattve iti sheShaH | dvitIyAdvivachanametat | 'antarA' vinA | viparItakrama ityanena krameNetyetaduktArtham, anyeShAM laya ityAdau grAhyam | tena sUtre laya iti sheSho darshitaH |
(2) siddhAntAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || vij~nAnamanastattve vinA viparItakrameNa laya ityuktaM netyarthaH | kuto netyataH pravR^ittam avisheShAdityetadvisheShadharmarahitatvAdityanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe - visheSheti | saN^kochakapramANAbhAvAdityarthaH | yadvA - vij~nAnamanastattvayoryathotpattilaya iti visheShapramANAbhAvAdityarthaH | nanu sarveShAmapi viparItakrameNaiva laya ityatrApi pramANaM nAsti | tathA cha sAmyamevetyato.apyAha - visheSheti| abhAvAditi vichChedaH| tathA cha sarvaM vA etatkramAdutpadyate kramAdvilIyata iti visheShapramANAbhAvAdityarthaH | nanu sarveShAmapi viparItakrameNaiva laya ityatrApi pramANaM nAsti | tathA cha sAmyamevetyatopyAha | visheSheti | AbhAvaditichChedaH | tathA sarvaM vA etatkramAdutpadyate kramAdvilIyata iti visheShapramA
NasadbhAvAdityartha | anena nAvisheShAdityaikapadyaM sUchitam | athavA - abhAvAdityeva ChedaH | tathAtve sarvaM vetyavisheShapramANAbhAvAdityarthaH ||
(3) nanvastyevoktaM liN^gadarshanaM keShAJNchitkramAllayaH, keShAJNchidvyutkramAdityatra visheShapramANarUpamataH kathaM visheShapramANAbhAva ityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - charAchareti || manasashcha vij~nAnamiti vyapadesha ityanena tadvyapadesha ityetat sa chAsau vyapadeshashcha tadvyapadesho mano vij~nAnamiti shabda iti vyAkhyAtam | 'charAchareShu' jaN^gamasthAvareShu | viShayasaptamIyam | idaM charAchareShu vyapadeshashchaJNchalAntaHkaraNAvabodharUpacharatattvarUpAcharaviShayako vyapadesha iti charAchareShvAlochanAditi chobhayAnvayi | pUrvatrAnvayena charAcharavyapAshrayovyapadesha ityetadvyAkhyAtam | charAchareShvAlochanAdvij~nAnaM bhavatItyanena cha tadbhAvabhAvitvAdityaMshaH tasmin charAcharaviShaye tasya manaso bhAvenAlochanena tasyAvabodhasya vR^ittij~nAnasya bhAvitvAt utpadyamAnatvAditi vyAkhyAtaH | yadvA - charAchareShvAlochanAdityanena chandrikArItyA charAcharavyapAshrayatvasya samAsAntargatatadbhAvaM pratyapi visheShaNatvaM j~nApitam | 'iti' hetorvyapadesho 'bhAgApekShayA syAt' indriyAvabodhAkhyabhAgaviShaya eva syAditi | anena 'bhajanaM bhAgasevayoH' iti vachanAt bhajadhAtorbhAve ktapratyaye niShpannabhaktashabdAt ktin pratyaye vA niShpannAdbhaktishabdAdvA tasyedamityaNi kR^ite niShpanno bhAktashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | 'na vij~nAnatattvApekShayA' na tattvaviShayo.apIti | anena turavadhAraNArtho.apyarthashchetyuktaM bhavati | yata evamato na liN^gadarshanavirodha iti vAkyasheShaH | anena - yadyapi 'manasashcha vij~nAnam' iti vyapadeshaH 'charAcharavyapAshrayaH' manorUpendriyatajjanyaj~nAnamanastattvavij~nAnatattvAkhyarAshidvayaviShayastatsAdhAraNaH | tathApIha yataH sa 'bhAktastu syAt' antaHkaraNavR^ittij~nAnAkhyabhAgaviShaya eva syAt, na tu manovij~nAnAkhyatattvaviShayaH, ato na tadvirodhaH | na chendriyAvabodhaviShayatve.apyanupapattiH | tattvayoriva tayorapi kAryakAraNAbhAvAyogAditi vAchyam | 'tadbhAvabhAvitvAt' teShu charAchareShu tasya manaso bhAvena | yadvA - charAcharavyapAshrayeNa tadbhAvenAlochanena tasya vR^ittij~nAnasya bhAvitvAdutpadyamAnatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati ||
(4) nanu 'manasashcha vij~nAnam' iti vyapadesho.astu bhAktaH, tathApi tattvaviShaya eva kiM na syAdityata Aha - skAnde cheti || chandrikArItyA smR^ityarthastu - 'avyaktaM' shrItattvAbhimanyamAnam avyaktAkhyatattvaM 'parAt' sarvottamAddharerutpannaM, 'mahAn' chaturmukhAbhimanyamAnaM mahattattvaM tu avyaktAdutpannam | tathAshabdaH samuchchaye | 'mahataH' chaturmukhAt mahattatvAbhimAninashchaturmukhAt vANyabhimanyamAnaM vij~nAnatattvaM samutpannam | vij~nAnatattvAdrudrAbhimanyamAnaM manastattvaM samutpannamiti | anena vaikArikAhaN^kArakAryasyApi manaso vij~nAnatattvakAryatvaM chAstIti j~nAyate | 'khAdikam' indriyAdyAkAshAdi vA | sarvasR^iShTAvayaM kramaH kimityA
shaN^kya netyAha -evamiti | yA 'bAhyA' brahmANDabahirjAtA sR^iShTiH saiva 'evaM' parAdityuktaprakAreNa bhavati | 'parA' mukhyA tAratamyaj~nApikA cha | atha yatra kvachittattvAnAmeva avarasya pUrvatvamityevaMrUpo viparItakramaH shrUyate, tatra kathamityatastasyA viShayamAha - antariti | 'viparItakramaH' parAdityuktApekShayA viparItakramotpattishrutiH 'prANAnmano manasashcha vij~nAnam' ityevamAdirUpA antaH brahmANDasya dehasya chAntastattvAbhivyaktau j~nAninAM tadAparokShye cha kramApekShayA cha pravR^ittetyarthaH | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - yasmAdavareShAM darshanAnte harerdarshanaM tasmAdutpattikramavadviparIto vyutkramo j~neya iti | vyaktipadaM darshanasyApyupalakShakam | ata eva TIkAyAmantarabhivyaktau j~nAninAM tattvAparokShye chetyuktam | AparokShyasya vyaktisAdhyatvAt | brahmANDasya dehasyachAntarvyaktAvAparokShye cha viparItakrama ityatra liN^gamAha - yasmAditi | yasmAddvArapAladarshanAnantaraM rAj~na iva adhamatattvadevatAdarshanAntaram 'ante' pashchAddhareH 'dR^ishiH' darshanaM bhavati darshanasAdhanIbhUtAdhamatattvadevatAvyaktishcha bhavati | tasmAdantastadvyaktyapekShayA viparItakrama ityuktaM yuktamityarthaH | chandrikAyAM tu smR^itikramApekShayA viparItakramashrutiH brahmANDAntaHsR^iShTyabhiprAyA | tattvadevAnAM dehotpattilakShaNAnusR^iShTyabhiprAyA | yadvA - viparItakramashrutiH j~nAninAM svadehe j~nAnikartR^ikatattvAbhimAnidevatAparokShyakramAbhiprAyetyuktam | tatpakShe vyaktishabdo dR^iShTiparaH | brahmANDasyAntardehasyAntardR^iShTiriti vyavasthayA.anvayaH| na tUbhayorubhayatrAnvayaH TIkAyAmabhivyaktAvityanantaram AparokShye cheti sheShaH | iti skAnda ityanvayaH | uktatvAditi sheShaH | asyAto manasashcha vij~nAnamiti vyapadeshaH, na tatvApekShayeti pUrveNAnvayaH | na kevalaM sUtra iti chashabdArthaH |
|| iti antarAdhikaraNam || 9 ||
|| 10. AtmAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe paramAtmanilayaviShayashrutivirodhaparihAraH kriyate | tatra sUtramupanyasya pUrvapakShaM sUchayan vyAchaShTe - neti || shruterityanena sUtre shruterityapipadachChedaH sUchitaH | paramAtmA.api lIyata iti netyarthaH | na kevalaM pR^ithivyAdirityApishabdArthaH | anena AtmA chetyanvitashchashabdo.apyarthatayA.api vyAkhyAtaH | tathA 'tamasi nilInaH' iti shruteH chetanatvayukteshcha paramAtmA.api lIyata iti sayuktikapUrvapakShashcha sUchitaH | sR^iShTyAdyaShTakakartR^itvarUpabrahmaliN^gapratipAdakaM 'sa idam' ityAdivAkyasheShodAharaNaM tu nilInashruterIshvaraikaviShayatvena niravakAshatvopapAdanAya | 'saH' eka eva paramAtmA 'idaM sarvaM' jagadvilApya 
chitprakR^itirUpodakAtmakena tamasA.a.achChAdya saMhR^itya svayaM 'vyuttiShThate' prAdurbhavati | atha sa idaM jagatsR^ijati | sR^iShTvA cha vividhaM 'sthApayati' sthitiM prApayati | atha 'vilApayati' saMhArayati 'prasthApayati' prerayati 'AchChAdayati' aj~nAnenAvR^itaM karoti 'prakAshayati' jIvakartR^ikAnubhavena jIvaM saMyojayati 'vimochayati' svaprApitabandhAdityarthaH | sarvatrAnvayArthaM sa iti dviruktiH | netyanena siddhAntapratij~nAyA uktatvAt tatrAshruteriti padachChedenoktaM hetuM yojayati - ashrutatvAditi | 'tadvilApya vyuttiShThate' ityAdyuktyodAhR^itashrutito.api brahmalayo neti j~nAyate | na chAnyato brahmalayaH shrutaH | ataH kasyAmapi shrutau brahmalayasyAshrutatvAdityarthaH | paramAtmanaH prakR^itatvAttallasyetyetAvatA pUrtau brahmetyuktiH kAlAparichChinnatvarUpayuktisUchanArthA |
(2) nanvantastamasi nilIna iti brahmalayasya shrutatvAtkathamuchyate ashrutatvamityata Aha - nilIneti || apihitatvamAchChAditatvam| upalakShaNametat| itarAdR^ishyatvamityapi draShTavyam | ata eva paiN^gashrutAvadR^ishyatvamuchyate | yathoktaM bR^ihadbhAShye -
laukikavyavahAro yo bhUbhArakShapaNAdikaH |
tadadR^iShTiM vinA chAnyo layaH kR^iShNAdinAM kvachit || iti ||
laukiko lokaviShayakaH | kuto nilInashabdo.apihitatvArthakaH, yenAshrutatvaM sidhyet ityatastaduttaratvenApi shruteriti ChedenoktAM shrutiM darshayati - tuchCheneti | shruteriti | samAkhyArUpashruterityarthaH | 'sa idaM sarvaM vilApya' ityAdeH 'vyuttiShThate' ityantasya 'nAsadAsIt' ityAdeH 'mahinA jAyataikam' ityantasya cha samarthanArthatvAditi bhAvaH | shruterityasya pUrveNAnvayaH | vyAkhyAteyaM shrutiH AnumAnikanaye | nilInatvamihApihitatvameva na tvanyaditi ||
atra na kevalaM samAkhyAnaM, kintu vAkyamapItyAshayena shruterityanenoktaM shrutivAkyaM chAha - sa iti || atra pUrvottaravAkyArthaparyAlochanayA vAkyalakShaNapramANena arthAt nilInashabdo.apihitArthe prayukta iti j~nAyate | kechidiyamapi prayogarUpashrutitvAtsamAkhyaiva, samAkhyAdInAmiti TIkA tu vastusthitikathanaparetyAhuH | 'saH' paramAtmA 'etasmin' prakR^itirUpe tamasi 'nilInaH' ChannaH svayaM prakR^itijIvakAlAnanupashyati enaM tu na ko.api pashyatItyarthaH | 'paiN^gishruteH' paiN^ginAM vAkyAt | asyApi nilInashabdeneti pUrvavAkyenA
nvayaH ||
(3) nanu kimarthamevaM nilInashruterarthAntaraM parikalpyate asyAH laya evArthaH kiM na syAt | na cha samAkhyAdivirodhaH | tasya shrutito durbalatvAt | na cha 'nityo nityAnAm' iti shrutyantarabalAttasyAH prAmANyopapatterityataH pravR^ittaM nityatvAchcha tAbhya ityaMsaM vyAchaShTe - nitya iti ||
nityo nityAnAM chetanashchetanAnAM
eko bahUnAM yo vidadhAti kAmAn |
tamAtmasthaM ye.anupashyanti dhIrAH
teShAM shAntiH shAshvatI netareShAm ||
iti kaThashruterayamarthaH - 'nityAnAM' svarUpataH avinAshinAM sakAshAt 'nityo' dehato.api nityaH paramanitya iti yAvat | nityAnAM nityatvaprada iti vA | evaM 'chetanAnAM' j~nAtR^INAmapi 'chetanaH' paramachetanaH, teShAM chaitanyaprada iti vA | yashcha svayameka eva 'bahUnAM' puruShANAM 'kAmAn' kAmyAn 'vidadhAti' karoti taM hR^idayasthaM ye dhIrAH anupashyanti teShAM 'shAshvatI' punarAvR^ittishUnyA 'shAntiH' mokSho bhavennetareShAmiti| 'sa nityaH' ityanyashrutivAkyam | saH paramAtmA dehato.api nityaH yato 'nirguNaH' sattvAdiguNAbaddho vibhuH paro vilakShaNo.ata ityarthaH | 'nityo vibhuH' ityanyA shrutiH | nityatve heturvibhurityAdikam | 'kAraNaH' kAraNaM jagata iti sheShaH | 'guNaiH' guNebhyassattvAdibhyaH 'paro' muktaH guNamayadehAdivarjitaH 'sarvadR^ik' sarvaj~naH 'shAshvato' nirvikAra ityarthaH | Adishabdena nityatvabodhakavAkyAntaraM gR^ihyate| tAbhya ityasya vyAkhyA shrutibhya iti| nityatvAditi | dehato.api nityatvAvagamAdityarthaH | brahmaNa ityanuShajyate | asyApi nilInashabdenApihitatvamuchyata iti pUrveNAnvayaH | chashabdo hetusamuchchaye | tathA cha bAhulyena 'nityaH' ityAdishrutInAM prAbalyAnnetarashrutivirodhena aprAmANyaM shaN^kyamiti taChrutivirodhAnnilInashruterarthAntarakalpanaM yuktamiti bhAvaH ||
|| iti AtmAdhikaraNam || 10 ||
|| 11. j~nAdhikaraNam || 
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvajanmaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate| sandehabIjaM shrutivirodhaM darshayati - nitya iti || na kevalaM parasyetyapishabdArthaH | nityatvamiti | avinAshitvamityarthaH | uktamiti | pUrvAdhikaraNodAhR^itavAkyeneti sheShaH | na chotpattishrutipratiyogyanAditvashruterevodAhartavyatayA nityatvashrutyudAharaNamasaN^gatameveti vAchyam | bhAvasya sataH nityatvoktyanupapattita eva prAgabhAvApratiyogitvarUpAnAditvasyApyuktaprAyatvAt | itIti | iti shrutyantareNetyarthaH | 'Atmano' jIvAH 'vyuchcharanti' mAtR^idehAt nissaranti jAyanta ityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha - ata iti | yata evaM shrutidvayena viruddhArthadvayamuktam, ataH shrutyorvirodha ityarthaH |
(2) anutpattij~nApakanityatvashrutyupanyAsenaiva jIvo.anutpattimAn prAgabhAvApratiyogitvarUpAnAditvAt Ishvaravaditi sayuktikapUrvapakSho labdho bhavatItyAshayavAn siddhAntayatsatramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || jIva ityanena jAnAtIti vyutpattyA j~no jIva iti j~nashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | pUrvasUtrAdanuvR^ittasya chashabdasyArtho.apIti | na kevalaM viyadAdiH kintu jIvo.apIti tasyArthaH | yadvA - nityatvenokto.apItyarthaH | ata ityanuvAdena parameshvarAditi vyAkhyAnam | parameshvarAdevetyevakArAnvayaH | sarvasUtreShu tasyaiva prakR^itatvAditi bhAvaH | utpadyata iti sUtre sheShoktiH | evakArasyAtrApyanvayaH | utpadyata ityAvartate | anena jIvo.api utpadyata eva, utpadyamAnashcheshvarAdeva utpadyata iti pratij~nAdvayaM sUchitaM bhavati | ubhayatra hetumAha - shabdAdeveti | anenAtashshabdasyAvR^ittissUchitA | na tatra pramANAntaraM gaveShaNIyamiti evashabdArthaH | tameva shabdamudAharati - ta iti | vAshabdo.avadhAraNe | 'te' prasiddhAH 'ete' jIvAH yataH 'chidAtmano' j~nAnasvarUpAH atassvarUpato.avinaShTAssanto 'jyotiH' prakAsharUpaM 'paraM' brahma nivishanti praLaye muktau cha | tarhi anAdinityatvashrutivirodha ityata Aha - avinaShTA iti | svarUpataH anAdinityA evetyarthaH | kAdAchitkanAso.api netyAha - neti | svarUpata iti sheShaH | 'kadAchana' mahApraLaye.anyadA vetyarthaH | iti shrutirityanantaram asti hIti sheShaH |
(3) nanvanAdinityasya jIvasyotpattiH shrutA.api kathaM yujyate vandhyAtvamabhyupagamya mAtR^itvavachanavat 
nityatvamabhyupagamya punarutpattivachanasya vyAhatatvAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - yukteshcheti || 'nityasyApi' anAdinityasyApi | apiH yadyapitathApItyarthe | anena sUtre j~nasyeti vipariNatamanuShajyate | cho.apyarthaH | sa cha visheShaNasamuchchayArtho.apItyuktaM bhavati | 'upAdhyapakSheyA' bAhyasharIrAkhyopAdhyutpattyapekShayA tadviShayakatayA utpattivachanaM yujyata ityarthaH | sharIrAderupAdhitvaM na pratiphalanAdhikaraNatvam, kintu utpattyAdirUpavikAravisheShApAdakatvam, ata evAha - utpattiriti | yujyata iti | anena nAyaM yuktishabdo liN^gArthaH, kintu yogArthako vivakShArthakashcheti sUchitam | sAvadhAraNaM chaitat | tena sautrachashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | avadhAraNena nedamupachAramAtram, kintu mukhyameva parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpatterevAtra vivakShitatvAditi sUchitam | anena - anAdinityasyApi j~nasya parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpatteH yogAnna taduktivyAghAta iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati ||
(4) atra smR^itisammatimAha - utpadyanta iti || chidAtmatvamanAdinityatve hetuH | tathA cha yadyapi yatashchidAtmAno jIvA ato.anAdinityAH, tathApi dehato.api nityAtparAtmana utpadyante| vyAhatimAshaN^kyAha - upAdhIti | bAhyopAdhyutpattyapekShayetyarthaH | 'teShAM' jIvAnAM, na kevalamanAdinityatvamityapishabdArthaH | vyomasaMhitAyAmityanantaraM nityasyApItyAdishabdenoktaM yuktamiti vAkyasheShaH ||
|| iti j~nAdhikaraNam || 11||
|| 12. utkrAntyadhikaraNam ||
(1) dharmiNi jIve utpattyanutpattishrutivirodhaparihArAnantaramatrAdhikaraNe jIvadharme parimANe.aNutvashrutivirodhaH parihriyate | tatra shrutivirodharUpaM saMshayabIjaM darshayati - vyAptA hIti || hishabdaH prasiddhau | 'AtmanaH' paramAtmarUpavisheShAH 'vyAptAH' paramamahatparimANAH 'chetanAH' j~nAnarUpAH 'nirguNAH' sattvAdiguNashUnyAH 'sarvAtmAnaH' sarvasyAdAnAdikartAraH 'sarvarUpAH' pUrNasvarUpAH | 'sarvaH pUrNaguNatvataH' ityukteH | 'anantAH' kAlato guNatashchAparichChinnA iti siddhAntarItyA shrutyarthaH | pUrvapakShe tvAtmashabdo jIvaparaH | visheShaNAni cha tasyaivetyAha - vyAptA hyAtmAna iti | samagrodAharaNaM tu siddhAntAnukUlatayA brahmaliN^gAni sUchayitum | vyAptatvaM deshato mahattvamiti yAvat | pratIyate | jIvasyetyanuShajyate | 'eShaH' iti shrutau hishabdaH prasiddhau | chAvanyonyasamuchchaye | tathA cha 'eSha AtmA' jIvo.aNuH yaM jIvaM ete 'sinIto' badhnItaH | ete ityetadeva vivR^iNoti - puNyaM cha pApaM cheti | atrApyaNurhyeSha AtmetyetAvadeva udAhartavye vAkyasheShoddhAro jIvatvaj~nApanArthaH | aNutvamityatrApi pratIyata ityanuShajyate | jIvasyeti chAsti | tataH kimityata Aha - ata iti | viruddhArthadvayapratItita evetyarthaH | 'virodhaH' shrutyoH pratIyata ityanuvartate ||
(2) yuktisahitavyAptatvashrutibalAt vyApta eva jIva iti pUrvapakShe siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya tachCheShameva 
pUrayati - ata iti || hetUnAmityuktirutkrAntyAdeH liN^gatAbodhanAya | tathApi vibhaktiM vinA hetutA.anavagamAttadarthaM sakAshAditi sheShaH kR^itaH| hetUnAmiti tu anuvAdo na doShaH| aNureveti tu prakaraNalabdhasAdhyoktiH | jIva iti vartate | tena sUtre j~na ityasyAnuShaN^gassidhyati | anena jIvaH aNureva na vyAptaH | kutaH? utkrAntigatyAgatimattvAt, patatrisharIravadityanumAnaprayogassUchitaH | na cha madhyamaparimANatvenAnyathAsiddhissyAt | tasyAnityatvaprasaN^gena nirAkR^itatvAditi bhAvenApyevakAraH prAyoji |
(3)à¤¼ vibhutvabAdhakAnAmaNutvasAdhakAnAM hetUnAmasiddhimAshaN^kya tatra tatsadbhAve shrutimAha - sa iti || sa jIvo bAhyasharIrabandhAdutkramyAmuM lokam 'adhigachChati' prApnoti | 'amuShmAdimaM lokaM' bhUlokaM pratyAgachChati | anantaraM 'sa garbhIbhavati' pUrvamagarbhaH, adhunA garbhassampadyate mAturudaraM pravishatIti yAvat| atha 'prasUyate' utpadyate| atha puNyapApasAdhanaM karma karotIti shrutyarthaH| shruterityanantaraM siddhAnAmiti sheShaH| asya hetUnAmityanenAnvayaH ||
(4) evamutkrAntyAdihetubhyo jIvasyAvyAptatve siddhe aNutvasAdhakAdhikaraNamadhye antarbhedAdhikaraNatvena kiJNchitprasaN^gAt chintyate| kimidamutkrAntyAdikaM jIvasya parameshvareNa? svayameveti| tatra pUrvapakShamAha - tatreti || 'so.asmAt' ityudAhR^itashrutAvityarthaH | tatretyAvartate | tasyotkrAntyAdAvityarthaH | jIvasyetyanuvartate | pratIterityasya svayamevetyanenAnvayaH | svayamevetyanantaraM tasyotkrAntyAdIti sAdhyamadhyAhAryam | neshvareNetyevashabdArthaH | nanvasyAM shrutau jIvasyotkrAntyAdyeva shrUyate, na tvanyAdhInatAvidhiH niShedho vA.asti | ato nAnayA dR^iDhanirNaya ityata Aha - eka iti | 'ekaH' svatantro 'jantuH' jIvaH 'prasUyate' utpadyate 'pramIyate' nashyati | evashabdasya dvirgrahaNaM sarvatrAnvayaj~nApakam | duShkR^itaM chetyanvitaH chashabdaH samuchchaye | anubhuN^kta ityatrApi sambadhyate | 'ityAdeH' evamAdismR^itivachanAchchetyarthaH | na kevalaM pratIteriti chArthaH | tathA cha smR^ityanusAreNa shruterapi jIvasyotkrAntyAdeH parAdhInatAniShedho.artha iti bhAvaH ||
(5) evaM pUrvapakShe tannirAkaraNAya sUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || 'sa etena' ityAdyekaM shrutivAkyam | 'eSha hyAnandam' ityanyat | anenottarayorityanena j~nApitaM vAkyadvayamudAhR^itaM bhavati | 'saH' jIvaH 'etena' svasthitena 'svAtmanA' svarUpabhUtamAnandamAdatte iti vyutpattyA svAtmashabdavAchyena paramAtmanA.anugR^ihitaH imaM mAtR^idehasthaM garbhaM pravishati | pareNaiva tatprerita eva jAyate | tenaiva lokAntaraM 'nIyate' mriyate 'unnIyate' mokShAyordhvaM nIyate | tametaM viShNuM svAtmetyabhivadanti vidvAMsa ityarthaH | anena svAtmashabdasya vidvadrUDhirdarshitA | 'eShaH' paramAtmA AnandaM jIvakR^itashubhakarmaphalam 'Adatte' gR^ihNAti svarUpAnandamanubhavatIti vA | 'abhi jIvayati' dhR^itaprANaM karoti saMsthApayati | 'udgamayati' dehAnnirgamayati UrdhvaM paralokaM gamayatIti vA | 'Agamayati' dehaM praveshayati | imAM bhUmimAgamayatIti vetyarthaH | yadyapyeShahyenaM jIvamityArabhyaiva dvitIyavAkyamudAhartavyam | tasyaiva prakR^itopayuktatvAt | tathApi dvitIyavAkye svAtmasha
bdAbhAvAt kathamuttarayorityanena dvitIyavAkyaM gR^ihyata ityAshaN^kyaM maivaM dvitIyavAkye svAtmashabdAbhAve.api tadvyAkhyAnarUpaiSha hyAnandamAdatta iti vAkyasadbhAvAditi bhAvena tatpUrvavAkyamapyudAhR^itam | ata eva sUtre ubhayodAharaNam | ityuttarayoriti | pauShyAyaNashrutau so.asmAditi vAkyApekShayottarayorityarthaH | sakAshAditi sheShaH| yadvA - saptamIyaM na ShaShThI | tathAtve sUtre vachanAditi sheShaH | bhAShye tUchyanta yata iti sheShaH | Adye tu bhavantIti | evaM hetuM vyAkhyAya idAnIM svAtmanA cheti pratij~nAMshaM vyAchaShTe - paramAtmanaiveti || svAtmanetyanuktvA paramAtmanetyuktyA paraM pUrNaM svarUpabhUtamAnandam Adatta iti vyutpattyA svAtmashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | utkrAntyAdaya ityanena sUtre utkrAntigatyAgataya iti pUrvasUtrAdvipariNatapadasyAnuvR^ittiH sUchitA | alpAkSharatvAyAdishabdaprayogaH | tathA cha so.asmAditi pUrvavAkyamapyetadarthakameva | smR^itistu prasavAdiduHkhAnubhave paramAtmadattasvAtantryamAheti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH ||
(6) uktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasyAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - neti || iti vyAptishruterityanenAtachChruteriti pUrvapakShahetvaMshasyANutvaviruddhavyAptatvashruterityartha ukto bhavati | bahuvachanashravaNAdiyaM shrutiH paramAtmani niravakAshA, utkrAntyAdikaM tu manogataM jIvAtmanyupacharyata iti bhAvaH | nANurjIva ityanena 'j~no.ataH' ityato j~na iti padAnuvR^ittyA pratij~nAMsho vyAkhyAtaH ||
(7) parihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || naitachChrutibalena jIvasya vyAptatvaM vaktavyamityarthaH | kuto netyatastatra tasyAH paramAtmaviShayatvena sAvakAshatvAditi hetUpaskAramabhipretya tadapi kuta ityAshaN^kAyAM tatra hetutvenetarAdhikArAdityaMshaM yojayati - sa iti | itIti | vAkya ityarthaH | yadvA - ityAdivAkyasyetyarthaH | iti paramAtmAdhikAratvAdityanenetarAdhikArAdityasyetarasyAdhikAraH, itarAdhikArastasmAt | yadvA - itaramadhikarotItItarAdhikAraH, bhAvapradhAnashchAyam | tathA cha 'saH' iti vAkye 'itarasya' prakR^itajIvAdbhinnasya paramAtmanaH 'adhikArAt' paThitatvAt prakR^itatvAditi yAvat | tata eva cha 'vyAptA hyAtmanaH' ityAdivAkyasandarbhasya 'itarAdhikArAt' paramAtmAdhikAratvAttatprakaraNatvAt| a evAsya 'vyAptAH' ityasya 'itarAdhikAratvAt' paramAtmaparatvAdityarthatrayamuktaM bhavati | tathA cha prakaraNabalAdvyAptA iti shrutirviShNuparaiva, na tu jIvaparA | na cha bahuvachanavirodhaH | paramAtmanyeva sa iti shrutAvAtmAna iti bahuvachanAntashabdaprayogeNAtratyabahuvachanasyApi tasminneva sAvakAshatvAt | nirguNA iti guNabandharAhityokteshcha | ata eva notkrAntyAdInAm aupachArikatvaM kalpyametachChruterabAdhakatvAditi bhAvaH | 'saH' paramAtmA 'idaM' jagat sR^ijati | so.antargato bahirgatashcheti dvidhA bhUtvA.antarbahishchedaM jagadbibharti | bahudhA bhUtvA idamanupravishya 'AtmanaH' svasya svata evAbhitaH Abhimukhyena nayati svakriyAnukUlakriyaM karoti | yadvA - 'AtmanaH' 
AtmarUpAnabhito nayati| 'sa AtmA sa AtmAnaH' tAdR^ishaikavachanabahuvachanAntashabdabodhyaH 'parovarIyAn' sarvottama iti shrutyarthaH | na chaivaM virodhaH paunaruktyaM vA, bahurUpatvAttAtparyaj~nApakatvAchcha | sR^iShTyAdikartR^itvAbhidhAyipUrvAMshasya 'sa IshaH' ityAdyuttarAMshasya chodAharaNametachChrutisthatachChabdAnAM viShNvaikaviShayatvasAdhanArtham | tadetatsarvamabhipretyoktaM tattvapradIpe - bahurUpairidaM jagatpravishya svata evAbhito nayati | sa AtmA sa AtmAnaH ityekasyaiva bahurUpatvaM punaH punastAtparyAdupadishati | viShNushrutiH sR^iShTyAdikartR^itvarUpatalliN^goktyA sa iti tachChabdAnAM viShNuviShayatvameveti sAdhayati | parovarIyastvoktyA chAtmashabditasya viShNoravaratvaM dUrIkarotIti |
(8) Ishvarasya bahuvachanavAchyatve bhedaH syAdityata Aha - ekashabdairiti || 'keshavaH' sR^iShTisaMhArayorbrahmarudraniyojako viShNureka evAbhinna evAnekarUpatvAt 'vedaiH' vedagataiH 'ekashabdaiH' ekavachanAntashabdairdvivachanAntashabdairbahuvachanAntashabdaishchochyate | tAvatA.asya viShNorbhinnatA nAshaN^khyetyarthaH | bhaviShyatpurANe ityanantaramuktam ato na bhedaprasiktidoSha iti vAkyasheShaH |
(9) ekasminnekashabdaprayogaM sampratipannasthale darshayati - taditi || vyAkhyAtametadvAkyaM prANanaye | aitareyashrutiH tadayamiti vAkyena paramAtmanaH ekasyaiva sharIrarathAdhiShThAtR^itvamuktvA tatra dvivachanayuktau mantrau pramANayati tadityanena | tattanmantrArthe mantradraShTR^iR^iShiNA hayagrIveNa pramANamuktamityarthaH | tanmantradvayaM paThati - Ateneti | ityAdIti | ityAdyudAharaNaM cha nirbhede.api harau bahurUpatvApekShayA bahuvachanaM yuktamityetamarthaM gamayatIti | tR^itIyAntapAThe ityAdinA karaNenaitamarthaM gamayatItyadhyAhAreNAnvayo draShTavyaH | na kevalaM bhaviShyatpurANoktimAtramiti chashabdArthaH | Adishabdena samagro mantraH 'nimiShashchit' iti mantrAntaraM cha gR^ihyate | tatra -
A tena yAtaM manaso javIyasA
rathaM yaM vAmR^ibhavashchakrurashvinA |
yasya yoge duhitA jAyate diva 
ubhe ahanI sudine vivasvataH || (R^i.10.39.12.)
iti prathamamantrasyAyamarthaH - he ashvinau AshugatimattvAddhayAsyatvAnnimittAdvA ashvishabdavAchyau viShNuvAyU 
'R^ibhavaH' sarvadevavAchako.ayaMshabdaH | tathA cha sarve devA yaM rathaM 'vAM' yuvayorarthe 'chakruH' kR^itavanto 'yasya' cha dehAkhyasya rathasya 'yoge' samyagyoge | nimittasaptamIyam | manovAkkAyakarmabhissaha bhagavadarpaNAkhyaikakriyAsambandhAt manovAkkAyakarmaNAM bhagavadarpaNAtteShAM tadadhInatvaj~nAnAt iti yAvat | 'vivasvato' vividhaM vAsavatvAt nimittAt tadvAchyAdviShNoH tatprasAdAt 'divo' ramAbhimanyamAnAyAH vidyAyAH 'duhitA' tajjanyaM sarasvatyabhimanyamAnaM viShNutattvAparokShaj~nAnaM jIvasya jAyate | tathA 'sudine' sAdhye ubhe ahanI jIvanmuktimuktyavasthe 'jAyete' bhavataH tena manasoà¤¼.api 'javIyasA' vegena manaso.api paTutareNa rathena adhyAtmaM dehAkhyena adhidaivaM prasiddharatharUpeNa rathena 'AyAtam' AgachChatamiti yathoktamaitareyabhAShye - R^ibhava iti devAnAM sAdhAraNaM nAma |
AdityA vasavo rudrAH vishve R^ibhava ityapi |
sarvadevasamAkhyA cha dvAdashAShTAdikeShvapi ||
iti shabdanirNaye | sukhaM dadata iti sudine | 'vivasvato' viShNossakAshAt divo duhitA ahanI cha jAyante | ahanI iti dvivachanena dvitvasiddhe.api ubhe iti vachanam adhyAtmAdhidaivayorubhayorapi vachanArthamiti | bhAgavatatAtparye tu - 'yatrobhayossashabdassyAt tatra dvivachane.apyubhe' ityuktam | 'sashabdaH' samAnashabdaH | kechittu - yasya manovAkkarmabhiH yoge bhagavatsambandhAditi vyAchakhyuH | tattu aitareyabhAShyataTTIkAviruddham |
nimiShashchijjavIyasA rathenAyAtamashvinA |
antiShadbhUtu vAmavaH || (R^i.8.62.2.)
iti dvitIyamantrasyAyamarthaH - he ashvinau 'nimiShashchit' chakShurnimeShAdapi 'javIyasA' atyantaM vegavatA dehAkhyarathenAyAtam | 'vAM' yuvayossakAshAt yat 'avaH' avanaM tat 'antiShat' samIpe vidyamAnam asmadantike sthitaM 'bhUtu' bhavitviti |
(10) yaduktaM vyAptishrutirIshvaraviShayA tatprakaraNAditi, tadayuktam, shrutyapekShayA prakaraNasya durbalatvAt, tanmAtreNa bahuvachanashruteH IshvaraviShayatvena saN^kocharUpabAdhAyogAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - sveti || iti vAkyasheSha iti| ityevaM rUpe kAShAyaNavAkyasheSha ityarthaH | shrutAbhyAmiti sheShaH | AtmashabdonmAnAbhyAmiti | AtmashabdonmAnatvaliN^gAbhyAmityarthaH | asya vyAptatvashruteH IshvaraviShayatvena sAvakAshatvAditi pUrvAdhyAhR^itavAkyenAnvayaH | na kevalam 'itarAdhikArAt' ityuktaprakaraNAt, kintu AtmashrutyunmAnatvaliN^gAbhyAM cheti chashabdArthaH | tathA cha shrutiliN^gasahitaprakaraNena kevalAyA bahuvachanashruteH bAdho yukta eveti bhAvaH | AtmashabdonmAnAbhyAmityanena sUtre svetishabdaH svashabdaH, svasya brahmaNaH shabda 
iti vA vigrahaH | tena cha tatparyAyAtmashabdo gR^ihyate | unmAnashabdashcha bhAvapradhAnaH | tena cha aparimitatvaliN^gamuchyate | 'paramatassetUnmAna' itivat ityabhipraiti | 'eShaH' iti shrutau uttarArdhena pUrvArdhoditamupapAdyate | tathA cha - 'eShaH' hariH 'hi' yataH guNaiH pUrNaH achintyashcha, tathA 'sa sarvavedaikayoniH' sarve vedAH ekaM kevalaM yonayo vyaktikAraNAni yasya sa tathoktaH sarvAdhIshaH sarvaj~naH sarvakartA cha, ato 'mAnashakteH' puruShagataparimANashakteH adhikatvenodgataH sarvebhyo guNAdhikatvena mAnashaktimatilaN^ghya vartate kaishchidapi na mAnashaktyA mIyata ityuktam | yadvA - 'mAnashakteH' vedagatayathArthaj~nAnajananashakterudgataH tadaviShaya ityarthaH | yadyapyevaM, tathApi 'asau' paramAtmA viShayatayA 'vedaiH pramitiM yAti' vedajanyaj~nAnaviShayo bhavatItyarthaH | aparimitasyApi vibhoH vedaiH ekadeshapramitiH tatprasAdAt bhavatIti bhAvaH | yadvA - vedAnAM svashaktyaviShayasyApi viShNoH tatprasAdAt j~nAnakaraNatvaM bhavatIti bhAvaH | atha vA - draShTushchakShuH itivat viShNuH pramitiM svapramitiM yAti yApayati svAtantryAdityarthaH | 
(11)à¤¼ AtmashruterunmAnatvaliN^gasya cha kuto vaiShNavatvamityata Aha - Atmeti || 'ameyaH' aparimitaH | smR^iteH viShNuviShayatvopapAdanAya paraMbrahmetyAdyupanyAsaH| ekapadamidaM, parAnandetyanantaraM visargalopaH ArSho bodhyaH| itishabdo.atrAdhyAhAryaH| ityAdikA evamAdyA abhidhA abhidhAyakAH shabdAH viShNumevaikaM mukhyato vadanti| 'AsAm' abhidhAnAm 'anyatra' jIvAdau kvachidapi 'gatiH' vR^ittiH mukhyato nAstItyarthaH | iti cha kaurme iti | na kevalaM vAkyasheShe shrutamAtrAbhyAM, kintu kaurme vachane viShNvekaniShThatvena nishchitAbhyAmapyAtmashabdonmAnAbhyAmityanvayaH | yadyapi 'vyAptA hyAtmAnaH' iti shrutAvAtmashabdAnantyayoH shravaNAt pR^ithagvAkyasheShagrahaNaM vyartham | tathApi 'vyAptA hyAtmAnaH' iti vAkye bahuvachanasamabhivyAhArAt anyArthatAyA eva jhaDiti pratibhAsAdvAkyasheShe cha tadabhAvenAsya smR^itigatAmeyapadavyAkhyeyodgatomAnashakteritipadayuktatvena cha nishchitArthatvAttadarthaM pR^ithagupanyAso yuktaH |
(12) nanvathApi na jIvasyANutvaM yuktam, aNostasya sharIraikadeshasthatvena tadanyatrAbhAvena kasyApyaprAptakaraNena kriyAnirvartakatvAbhAvena sarvasharIragatasparshaj~nAnAyogAt tatra tatra chakShurAdiShu taistairyugapadrUpAdiparij~nAnAyogAchchetyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - avirodha iti || aNorapi jIvasyetyAdinA sUtre j~nasya jIvasyetyasyAnuvR^ittyA virodhapadAvR^ittyA cha yato jIvasya aNutvavyAptyavirodhaH aNutve.apyaMshaiH sarvasharIravyAptiryujyate, ato 'virodhaH' tatra tatra parij~nAnayogAkhyavirodho neti yojanA darshitA | apistu yadyapitathApItyarthaH, samuchchayArtho vA | ubhayAdR^iShTibAdhaparihArAya pravR^ittaM chandanavaditi dR^iShTAntAMshaM chandaneShu

(13) nanu niyAmakaM vinA na dR^iShTAntamAtreNa arthasiddhiH, etatpratikUladR^iShTAntasyApi vachanasambhavAdityata Aha - aNumAtro.apIti || aNuparimANo.apItyarthaH | apiH pUrvoktArthakaH | aMshairiti sheShaH | 'sharIrANi' sharIrAN^gAni 'harichandanavipruSho' gandhadravyabindavaH ekadeshapatitAH tiShThanti, tatheti sheShaH | brahmANDapurANe uktamiti sheShaH | tathA cha asyaiva niyAmakatvAnnoktadoSha iti bhAvaH |
(14) uktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasyAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - avasthitIti || vipruSha ityanuShajyate | tathA neti vApyatrAnvIyate | sarvasharIravyAptiriti chAsti | tathA cha chandanasya vipruShaH sarvasharIravyAptiryujyate | kutaH? (15) parihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || na jIvasya sharIre samyagasamyagavasthAnAbhAva ityarthaH | yena dR^iShTAntavaiShamyaM syAditi bhAvaH | kuto netyatastatra hetutayA abhyupagamAdityaMshaM yojayati - jIvasyeti || anena sUtre j~nasya jIvasyetyasya anuvR^ittissUchitA | na kevalaM chandanabindoH kintu jIvasyApItyaperarthaH | 'tathA.abhyupagamAt' chandanabinduvaddehe hR^idayataditarasthAnayoH samyagasamyagavasthAnAbhyupagamAt | kathametat 'tathA.abhyupagamAt' chandanabinduvajjIvasyApi sAMshatvAbyupagamAdityarthaH | na chAnityatvaprasaN^gaH | yato na sAMshatvamAtramanityatve prayojakam, kintvArambhakAMshavattvaM, tachcha na jIve.asti| anyathA prakR^ityAderapi dashadiksambandhena sAMshatvAdanityatvaprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | ayaM cha bhAvastattvapradIpe sUchitaH | kutastathA.abhyupagama ityatastatra hetutayA hR^idi hItyaMshaM yojayati - hR^idIti | shruteriti sheShaH | hR^idi hIti shrutipratIkagrahaNam | hR^idaye.avasthitivaisheShyAbhyupagamAditi sthaloktirUpaM vA | 'hi' yataH 'eShaH AtmA' jIvo 'hR^idi' hR^idaye svarUpeNAsti ato nendriyavR^ittiM vinA.aNostasya viShayasaN^gatiriti ShaTprashnashrutivAkyArthaH | anena - 
chandanavajjIvasya 'avirodhaH' svarUpatadaMshAbhyAM sarvasharIravyAptiryujyate | kutaH? chandanabindorAtmanassakAshAt 'avasthitivaisheShyAt' sharIraikadeshe samyagavasthAnasya anyatra asamyagavasthAnasya cha visheShasya anubhavasiddhatvAdasya cha jIve.abhAvAditi chet - na, kutaH? jIvasyApi hR^idi tadanyatra cha tathAbhAvAbhyupagamAt | so.api kutaH? 'hR^idi hi' iti shruteriti sUtrayojanA virodhapadAnuvR^ittyA naJNAvR^ittyA tathAshabdAdhyAhAreNa cha darshitA bhavati | idaM tvavadheyam - sAMshAnAM devAdInAmekasmin dehe hR^idi navanItapiNâDavatsAndradravyarUpeNa samyagavasthAnaM tadanyatrAsamyagavasthAnamiti | yathoktaM bR^ihadbhAShye -

(16) evaM svarUpatadaMshAbhyAM AtmanaH sharIravyAptyavyAptI sadR^iShTAntamuktvA prakArAntareNApi tadupapAdakaM sUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - guNAdveti || yathA Alokasya pradIpasya prakAshAkhyaguNeneti | anenAlokasyAlokaguNena vyAptivaditi dR^iShTAntAMsha AvR^ittyA vyAkhyAtaH | 'jyotIrUpeNa' pradIparUpeNa 'avyAptiH' dIpikAdAveva samyagavasthAnam anyatra tadabhAva ityarthaH | 'chidguNena' j~nAnAkhyaguNeneti | anena paJNchamI tR^itIyArthe guNavyAptimapekShyeti lyablopanimittetyuktaM bhavati | sharIrAN^geShu hR^idi cha vyAptiravyAptiriti | anena sUtre j~nasyAvirodha iti padAnuShaN^geNA.aNorapi jIvasya vyAptyavyAptyavirodha iti dArShTAntikAMsho vyAkhyAtaH | iti vetyanantaramavirodha itipadamanuShaJNjanIyam | evaM vA virodhaparihAraH kArya ityarthaH | anena - jIvasya guNino.aNutve.api 'Alokavat' pradIpaprakAshavat guNAt chidguNasya vyAptiyogAdavirodhaH | na tatra tatra parij~nAnAyogAkhyavirodha iti vetItishabdAdhyAhAreNa sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(17) nanvavirodhasUtroktAMshavyAptiH guNAdvetyuktaprakAshavyAptishchaikatra viruddhetyata Aha - skAnde cheti || yathA.avirodhastathoktamiti sheShaH | chashabdo vachanAntarasamuchchaye | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - na kevalaM 
skAnde, kintvanyatra cheti | kimuktamityatastatpaThati - asamyagiti | 'hi' yataH 'surAH' devA asamyaksamyagityavasthAbhedata ekasminneva sharIre hR^idayAditarasthAneShvaMshairasamyagavasthAnaM, hR^idaye tu aMshisvarUpeNa samyagavasthAnamityavasthAbhedamapekShyaiva vyAptyavyAptiyutAH, evaM devAMshA arjunAdayoà¤¼.api pratyekaM hR^idayAditaratrAsamyaktasmiMshcha samyagavasthAnena vyAptyavyAptiyutAH | evamaMshyapekShayA.apyavyAptiyutAH asamyagavasthitAshchAMshinastvaMshApekShayA samyagavasthitAH vyAptiyutAshcha, na tvanyathA | devAdibhyo.anye narAstu prakAshaguNenaiva vyAptiyutAH, na devavatsAndravyAptibhAjaH | ato jIvAnAmaNutve.api na tatra tatra parij~nAnAyogAkhyavirodhAvakAsha ityarthaH |
(18) nanvastu guNasya vyAptiH, guNinaH kuta ityata Aha - chidguNasyeti || j~nAnAkhyaguNasyetyarthaH | 'svarUpatvAt' anapAyitvena guNyabhinnatvAt | tadvyAptirityAvartate | tathA cha 'tadvyAptiH' guNavyAptiH guNivyAptirbhavati | tarhi kathaM vyavahArabheda ityato.apyAha - tadvyAptiriti | guNavyAptirguNavyAptishcheti vyavahArabhedo.api yujyate | kutaH? 'chidguNasya svarUpatvAt' savisheShAbhinnatvAt | samyagasamyagavasthAbhedena vyAptyavyAptiyuktatvaM cha na deveShu sarvatraikavidhamityAha - shaktiyogAditi | 'surANAM' devAnAM tu 'shaktiyogAt' gandharvAdibhyo.adhikashaktyAkhyAdupAyAttebhyaH utkR^iShTA vyavasthitiH yuktA | deveShvapi keShAJNchidadhamebhyo.adhikashaktiyogAdichChayA samyagavasthAnaM vyAptishchAbhyadhikA | teShAmityukteH avatAreShvapi sauShThavasArvaj~nasaulakShaNyAdiguNAH paridR^ishyamAnAH yujyante | yathA madhvAchAryavaryANAmiti | evaM 'vividhA' nAnAvidhA 'vyavasthitiH' vishiShTAvasthAvasthAnaM yuktamevetyarthaH | na chaivam 'aNUnAmapi jIvAnAM prakAsho vyApako bhavet | aNDamAtre bahishchApi devatAnAM yathAkramam' iti mANDUkabhAShyavirodhaH| tatra devAnAM prakAshavyAptyukteriti vAchyam| devatAnAM jIvAnAmiti sAmAnAdhikaraNyena asya vAkyasya devamAtraparatve.api devAnAm aMshaparityAgena kevalaM prakAshavyAptyabhAve.api aMshasahabhAvena prakAshavyApterapi sattvAt | yadvA - prakAshashabdaH aMshasyApyupalakShakaH | mAtrashabdo.avadhAraNArthaH | tathA cha aNUnAmapi jIvAnAM devetareShAmaNDamAtre yathAkramaM prakAsho vyApakaH | ata eva tattvapradIpe - 'tadyathAhANunashchakShasaH prakAsho vyAtata evamevAsya puruShasya prakAsho vyAtataH' (shANDilya.) iti shrutimudAhR^itya jIvamAtrasya sharIrAdbahirapi prakAshavyAptirastItyuktam | atAttvikadevAnAmaNDamAtre yathAkramamaMsho vyApakaH | tAttvikadevAnAM tu yathAkramaM bahirapi aMsho vyApaka ityubhayaparaM vAkyamiti na virodhaH |
|| iti utkrAntyadhikaraNam || 12 ||
|| 13. vyatirekAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaNe jIvasyaikarUpatvAnekarUpatvaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate | sandehabIjaM shrutivigAnaM darshayati - sa iti || 'saH' jIvo nityaH | tatra hetuH - yato niravayava iti | tatraiva hetvantaram - puNyayukpApayukcheti | tatphalabhoktatyarthaH | tathA cha nityatvAbhAve kR^itahAnAkR^itAbhyAgamaprasaN^gAttadeShTavyamiti bhAvaH | ata eva teShAM baddhakramatvAnna pR^ithak tachChabdAbhAvaH | 'imaM' bhUlokaM 'pratyAvartate' puNyapApakShaye punaH punarAgachChati | evamamuM paralokaM 'pratyAvartate' tadA tadA gachChati 'sa vimuchyate' bandhAt | 'sa ekadhA bhavati' ekarUpa eva bhavati | nAnekarUpa jIvatvaj~nApanAya, niravayavatvAdaMshabAhulyenApyanekarUpatvaM na sambhavatIti pUrvapakShayuktij~nApanAya cha shruterIshvaraviShayatvanivAraNAya 'puNyayuk' ityAdivAkyasya, 'sa nityaH' iti tadAdivAkyasya chodAharaNaM kR^itam | ekasya jIvasyeti sheShaH | 'abahutvam' abahurUpatvam ekarUpatvamiti yAvat | sa jIvaH 'paJNchadhA' paJNcharUpaH | evamuttaratrApi | 'gachChati' paraM lokaM prati | atrApi jIvatvaj~nApanAya 'sa muchyate' iti sheShodAharaNam | atra shrutidvaye.api pratipAdyo yogijIvaH | sa eveha vichAraviShaya iti dhyeyam |
(2) sayuktikAbahurUpatvashrutivirodhena bahurUpatvashruteH aprAmANyAttatsAmyAjjagatkAraNatvashruteH aprAmANyAt na harau shrutisamanvayo yukta iti prApte siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - ata iti || yato virodho dvedhA shrutimUlakaH saMshayabIjamasti, ataH saMshayanivR^ittyai taM virodhaM pariharati sUtrakR^idityarthaH | sUtraM vyAchaShTe - yatheti || yathA 'gandhaH' guNaH vAyunA.a.akR^iShTaH puShpAt puShpaM vihAya 'pR^ithak' pArthakyena pradeshAntarasthitaM ghrANadeshaM gachChati tathA ye yogijIvAMshAH aMshino jIvAt pR^ithagvibhaktAH santastatra tatra svakAryAya gachChantItyarthaH | yadvA - gandhashabdo gandhavaddravyAvayavaparaH | ata eva prameyadIpe 'vAyurgandhAniva' ityatra gandhavato.avayavAniti vyAkhyAtam | pR^ithagityanena vyatirekashabdasya pR^ithagbhAvArthatvamabhipraiti | aMshinoM.ashA ityanena sUtre j~nasyeti vipariNatapadasyAnuvR^ittiraMshairityadhyAhArashcha sUchitaH | ata eva TIkAyAm - prAthamyasAmyena guNatvoktirityuktam | etena 'yathA gandhasya bhUmeshcha na bhAvo vyatirekataH' iti 
tR^itIyaskandhavirodho.api nirastaH | na chaivaM dIpaM vihAya vR^itterdravyatvasAdhakatAvivAdAditi pUrvAdhikaraNaTIkoktyA gandhAdiguNAnAmapi guNinaM vihAya gamanAvagamanAt tathA dravyatvasAdhakagamanadUShakachandrikayA cha virodha iti vAchyam | gamanokteH sUkShmAvayavaviShayatvAt, dUShaNokteshcha sthUlAvayavaviShayatvAt, pakShadvayasyApyaviruddhatvAt | atra bhAShyaTIkayoH AlokagandhayorguNatvoktirmukhyA | dravyatvoktistvamukhyeti draShTavyam |
(3) nanu vibhaktAMshabAhulyena jIvasya bahurUpatvAbhyupagame.api 'sa ekadhA' (gaupavana.) iti shrutivirodha ityatastatra tasyAH svarUpaikyaviShayatvAditi parihAram, na cha bhinnAMshashUnyatvAdanekarUpatvAnupapattirityatastatra yoginAmapi bahurUpatvashakteH yogArAdhiteshvaraprasAdAyattatvAditi parihAram, na cheshvarasyApyetadashakyamityatastatra tasyAchintyashaktitvAditi parihAraM chAbhipretya kuta etatsarvaM j~nAyata ityatastatra pramANapradarshakatayA tathA cha darshayatIti sUtrakhaNDo yojya ityAshayena tatsUchitashrutimudAharati - atheti || prameyAntarArambhArtho.athashabdaH | jIvaH svarUpata eka eva san 'gandhaguNavadvyatirichyate' aMshinaM vihAyAMshaiH pR^ithagbhavati 'athaikIbhavati' punaH punaraMshairaikyaM sampadyate | atha yogasampadA bahvIbhavati bahurUpassampadyate | 'taM' jIvaM 'yathA yathA' ekadhA.anekadhA cha, tathA tathA bhavati jIvaH | IshvaraH achintyashaktiH kutaH | yataH 'paramo' lokottaro 'garIyAn' gurutamo mahattamaH ityarthaH | atraika evetyuktyA svarUpaikyamuktam | sampadA bahurUpatvamuktam | tamityAdinA yoginAM bahurUpatvashakteH yogArAdhiteshvaraprasAdAdhInatvamuktvA tatsAmyaM nirAkR^itam | so.achintyashaktiritIshvarasthAchintyashaktitvoktyA IshvarasyApyashakyamidamityAshaN^kA nivAritA | paramo garIyAnityanena lokavirodhaH parihR^itaH | shrutirityanantaramuktArthe pramANamiti sheShaH |
(4) bhinnAMshashUnyatvasya yogasampadA ityasya cha shrutau kaNThato.anuktestadartham atrArthe chashabdasUchitAM smR^itiM darshayati - achintyayeti || svarUpata eka eva jIvaH 'avayavavarjito' bhinnAMshashUnyo.api achintyayeshvashaktyA prAptayA 'yogasampadA' yogashcha sA sampachcha paramayogashAstroktayogAkhyasampadA achintyashaktIshvaraprasAdAgatadhyAnopAyAkhyasampattyA svAtmAnaM bahudhA kR^itvA krIData ityarthaH | 'etena yogaH' ityatretarayogashAstrasyaiva dR^iShTArthaviShaye aprAmANyamuktaM bhagavatA, na tu paramayogasyeti tattvapradIpa evoktam | iti pAdme ityanantaraM sUtrakR^iduktamuktamiti sheShaH |
|| iti vyatirekAdhikaraNam || 13 ||
|| 14. pR^ithagadhikaraNam ||
(1) asminnadhikaraNe jIvasya paramAtmAbhinnatvAdiviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate | saMshayabIjaM shrutivigAnaM darshayati - tattvamasIti || 'ityAdiShu' evamAdishrutivAkyeShu | Adishabdena 'sa yo ha vai tatparamaM brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati' (muM.3.2.9.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | 'pareNa' paramAtmanA | 'nityo nityAnAm' ityatra 'chetanashchetanAnAm' ityatra cha nirdhAraNaShaShThyA jIvasya bhedaH pratIyate | 'dvA suparNA' ityatra tu abhedavirodhidvitvasaN^khyayA bhedavAchakadvishabdenaiva vA bhedo.avagamyata iti dhyeyam | 'tattvamasi' ityetadAnandamayAdhikaraNe, 'nityo nityAnAm' ityetat 'nAtmA' ityatra, 'dvA suparNA' ityetat dyubhvAdhikaraNe vyAkhyAtam |
(2) 'tattvamasi' ityAdishruteH ShaDvidhatAtparyaliN^gopetatvena prabalatvAt paramAtmabhinna eva jIva iti pUrvapakShe siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || upadeshAdityasyArthaH shruteriti | nanvabhedashruterabhinno jIva ityapi suvachatvAdavadhAraNAnupapattirityataH sopapattiketi hetuvisheShaNamadAyi | viruddhadharmAdhikaraNatvarUpayuktiyukteryarthaH | sAvadhAraNasya pR^ithagiti sAdhyapadasyArtho bhinna eveti | svAtmanetiprakR^itaparamAtmana iti sheShaH | j~na ityasya anuvR^ittapadasyArtho jIva iti | shrutisUtrayoH pratij~nAvAkyAditve.api hetugarbhA pratij~nA.api upapattij~nApiketi pramANalakShaNokteraniyamapakShamAshritya hetugarbhapratij~naiveha pradarshitA | evamanyatrApi draShTavyam | yataH 'paraH' paramAtmA.achintyaH sAkalyena 'jIvasaN^ghAt' jIvasamudAyAt 'paramaH' uttamaH pUrNaH guNaiH | jIvasaN^ghastu chintyaH paramatvAvadhibhUto.apUrNashcha 'hi' prasiddhaH | kiJNcha - yato.asau harirnityamuktaH, ayaM jIvashcha saMsarati bandhAnmokShaM tataH paramAdeva svasyAbhivAJNChati 'hi' prasiddham | ato jIvaviruddhadharmatvAt tato bhinna eveti shrutyarthaH | yadyapi shrutAvIshvaradharmikabhedasyaiva shravaNAt 'jIvaikyaM paramAtmanaH' ityanuvyAkhyAne tathaivoktatvAchcha Ishvaro jIvAdbhinna iti pratij~nAtavyam | tathApi jIvapeTikAtvAdekavittivedyatayA viruddhadharmoktidvArA jIvadharmikabhedasyApi shrutyuktitvAdevamuktam | ata eva sudhAyAM - yato viShNuH jIvAt jIvashcha viShNoH pR^ithagiti sAdhyanirdeshaH kR^itaH |
(3) nanvevaM sati 'tattvamasi' ityAdyadvaitashruternirviShayatayA.aprAmANyaM syAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - taditi || j~nAnAnandAdibrahmaguNA evetyuktyA abhedetyuktyA cha taditi tachChabdadvayena 
svAtmaneti prakR^itasya paramAtmanaH parAmarshaH, tasya guNAstadguNA iti vigrahaH, tadguNashabdastadguNasadR^ishaguNaparaH, dvitIyatachChabdo bhAvapradhAna iti cha sUchitam | asyetyanena j~nasyeti vipariNatapadasya sUtre.anuvR^ittissUchitA | na chAyogyasya jIvasya j~nAnAnandAdiguNAbhAva iti vAchyam | asya shAstrasya vishiShTAdhikArikatvena taM pratyeva 'tattvamasi' ityAdyupadeshapravR^itteH asya sajjIvasyetyarthAbhyupagamAt | sArapadamanUdya vyAchaShTe - sAraH svarUpamiti | na cha j~nAnAnandAdirUpabrahmaguNAnAM kathaM jIvasvarUpatvamiti vAchyam | brahmaguNA ityasya tadguNasadR^ishaguNA ityarthAbhyupagamAt | evaM sUtre.api guNashabdastadguNasadR^ishaguNaparaH | ata iti sAvadhAraNam | anena sautratushabdo vyAkhyAtaH | tadvyapadesha ityasya paryavasitArtho.abhedavyapadesha iti | 'tattvamasi' ityAdiparabrahmaikyoktirityarthaH | j~nAnAnandAdItyAdivAkyaM cha yato jIvasya brahmaguNasadR^ishaguNasvarUpatvam, atastadvivakShayaiva gauNyA vR^ittyA jIve brahmAbhedoktiH abhedaprApakatadAdipadaprayogo, na tvabhedAbhiprAyeNa | yata evamabhedavyapadesho.anyathopapannaH, ato na tasyAprAmANyamiti sAdhyAdhyAhAreNAvR^ittyA yojyam | evaM yatastadvyapadesho jIvasya tadguNasAratvamapekShyopapanno.ato nAbhedashruteraprAmANyamiti pratij~nAdhyAhAreNa sUtrayojanA draShTavyA | sarvaguNAtmakatvAditi | samastajagadguNasadR^ishaguNasvarUpatvamapekShya yathA 'sarvaM khalvidaM brahma' iti Chandogashrutau prakR^iShTaj~nAtR^itvAnnimittAt prAj~nashabdoktasya brahmaNaH 'sarvAtmakatvaM' jaDajagabhedaH 'uchyate' vyapadishyate tathaivetyarthaH | yathetyAdinA praj~na eva prAj~naH tadvat tasya sarvAbhedoktivaditi dR^iShTAntAMsho vyAkhyAtaH | yadyapi ChandogabhAShye 'idaM brahmAtisAmIpyAt sarvaM pUrNaguNatvataH' iti vachanAnusAreNedaMsarvapadayoH paramAtmani mukhyavR^ittirabhihitA, na tu gauNI vR^ittiH | tathApi padasamanvayAbhiprAyeNa tasya pravR^ittatvAt, vAkyAnvayAbhiprAyeNAtra gauNavR^ittyabhidhAnAt na virodhaH |
(4) atraiva smR^itisammatimAha - bhaviShyaditi || na kevalaM sUtrakR^itA sUtra evaitaduktam, kintu spaShToktirUpe bhaviShyatpurANe choktamityarthaH | kimuktamityatastatpaThati - bhinnA iti | yadyapi jIvAH paramAtmano bhinnAH, paramAtmA.api jIvebhyo bhinnaH | tathApi sarveShu 'vedavAdeShu' 'tattvamasi' ityAdiShu 'brahmarUpeNa' parabrahmAbhedena 'prochyante' vyapadishyante | kasmAt? 'j~nAnarUpataH' tadupalakShitabrahmaguNasadR^ishaguNasvarUpatvAdityarthaH | anena jIvabrahmAbhedokteH chittvAdisAmyaM nimittamityuktaM bhavati | iti bhaviShyatpurANe itItishabdAnvayaH |
|| iti pR^ithagadhikaraNam || 14 ||
|| 15. yAvadadhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvanityatvaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate | saphalaM pUrvapakShamAha - jIvasyeti || j~no.ata ityatreti bhAvaH | na kevalaM viyadAdeH, kintu jIvasyApIti vA, na kevalaM jIvopAdheH kintu jIvasyApIti vA.aperarthaH | na kevalaM pUrvoktanyAyenotpattimAtraM jIvasya, kintu utpattimato bhAvasya vinAshitvarUpAnityatvaniyamAdanityatvamapi prAptamityapishabdAbhiprAyaH | anena sayuktikapUrvapakShaH pradarshitaH | tataH kimityata Aha - ata iti | itishabdAnantaraM shruta iti sheShaH | tathA cha yatastasya jIvasyotpattimattvaM, vinAshitvaprAptirUpAnantyAvAptirmuktishcha na yujyata iti yojanA | anena pUrvapakShaphalaM darshitam | 'saH' jIvaH | anAdinetyetat bandhakapuNyapApayorubhayorapi visheShaNam | pareNetyetat paramAtmanA baddhaH, pareNa bandhAdbandhakakarmaNA nirmuktaH, ityubhayatrAnveti | 'AnantyAya' avinAshAya mokShAya 'kalpyate' samartho bhavati | tatprApnotIti shrutyarthaH |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || paramAtmetyanena Atmashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | 'tiShThati' ityanena bhAvishabdaH | 'anAdyanantatvena' utpattinAshashUnyatveneti sattvaprakAra uktaH | 'evaM' tAvatkAlaM jIvo.api tiShThatItyanena sUtre j~na ityanuvR^ittissUchitA | na kevalaM paramAtmA kintu jIvo.apIti samuchchaye apishabdaH | anena bimbasya paramAtmano.anAdyanantatvAt jIvasvarUpopAdheshcha yAvadAtmabhAvitvAt paramAtmano.anantatvena bimbopAdhisannidheranAdyanantatvAt nityatvAditi hetusamuchchAyakatayA sautrachashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | na doSha iti sAdhyAMshaH anAdikarmasambandhaH AntyAvAptishcha na yujyata ityukto doSho neti pUrvapakShaphalakathanaparabhAShyeNaiva vyAkhyAtaprAyatvAt punarna vyAkhyAtaH | anenaiva 'so.anAdinA' iti shrutyaprAmANyadoSho.api netyapi vyAkhyAtaH |
(3) kuta etadakhilaM siddhamityataH tatra pramANapradarshakatayA taddarshanAditi sUtrakhaNDaM yojayati - nitya iti|| bimbabhUtaH 'paraH' paramAtmA nityaH | tathA 'jIvaH' pratibimbanopAdhibhUtaH jIvasvarUpaprakAsho 'nityo' yAvatparamAtmabhAvI | na chaivaM 'brahman layamabhyupaiti' iti jIvasya brahmaNi layashrutivirodha ityAha - anityA iti | yatastasya jIvasya 'dhAtavo' bAhyadehAH anityAH ato jIvA utpadyante 'mriyante' nashyanti ityuchyante | tathA cha shruterupAdhiviShayatvAt na tadvirodhaH iti bhAvaH | svarUpato.avinAshitvAdeva jIvo dehabandhAt 'vimuchyate' AnantyAvAptirUpamuktibhAgI cha bhavatIti shrutyarthaH | chashabdaH kriyAsamuchchaye |
(4) sUtre darshanAchchetyapi chashabdAnvayena sUchite smR^itI darshayati - Atmeti || sukhaduHkhapadAbhyAM bAhyopAdhirupalakShyate | ata eva TIkAyAm - dhAtvAdipadoditetyuktam | bhArate Atmeti pAdaH ekasthAnasthitaH | Atmetyasya sukhaduHkhetyasya cha vyAkhyAnarUpo jIvadhAtupadaghaTito.anyaH pAdaH sthalAntaragataH | ata eva na punaruktiH | dhAtustvityanvayaH | ubhayatrApi tushabdo vailakShaNyadyotakaH | bhArata ityanantaraM vachanamiti sheShaH | AgniveshyashrutivachanamityubhayatrApi yata iti sheShaH | asyaivaM jIvo.apIti pUrveNAnvayaH | chashabdaH shrutismR^itisamuchchayArthaH |
|| iti yAvadadhikaraNam || 15 ||
|| 16. puMstvAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvasya AnandAdirUpatvatadabhAvashrutyorvirodhaH parihriyate | shrutivirodharUpaM sandehabIjaM darshayati - vij~nAnAtmeti || 
vij~nAnAtmA saha devaishcha sarvaiH prANA bhUtAni sampratiShThanti yatra | 
tadetadakSharaM vedayate yastu somya sa sarvaj~naH sarvamevAvivesha ||
iti ShaTprashnashrutiH | 'sa AnandaH' iti shrutyantaram | itIti | ityAdishrutibhirityarthaH | somyeti kasyachitsambodhanam | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | tathA cha 'vij~nAnAtmA' vij~nAnasvarUpo jIvaH 'prANAH' chakShurAdyAH tadviShayAshcha rUpAdayaH 'bhUtAni' pR^ithivyAdIni tanmAtrAshcha 'sarvairdevaiH' abhimAnibhiH sUryAdibhiH saha 'yatra' yasmin akShare brahmaNi sampratiShThanti | tadetadakSharaM yaH puruSho 'vedayate' vijAnAti 'saH' uktaprakAreNa sarvaj~naH 'sarvaM' pUrNaM paraM brahma 'Aviveshaiva' dhruvamAvishatyeveti prathamashrutyarthaH | 'saH' jIvaH 'AnandaH' AnandarUpaH | evaM balarUpaH ojorUpaH 'pareNa' paramAtmanA.amumAmuShmikaM lokaM prati nIyate | tatpUrvaM tenaiva dehasambandhAdvimuchyata iti dvitIyashrutyarthaH | AnandAdiguNAnAM pratyekamabhede tAtparyaj~nApanArthaM sa ityabhyAsaH | sa pareNetyadhikAMshodAharaNam asya IshvaraviShayatAnirAsAya | evaM pUrvavAkyasyApi 'prANA bhUtAni' ityuttaravAkyabalAt IshvaraviShayatA nirAkAryA | 'saH' jIvaH | AnandIbhavatItyekaM padam | pUrvamanabhivyaktAnandarUpo muktAvabhivyaktAnandarUpaH sampadyata ityarthaH | aj~nAnAdabalAditichChedaH | j~nAnIbhavati balIbhavatItyasyApi ukta evArthaH | kechittu - itaH paramAnandavAn j~nAnavAn bhavatIti inipratyayAntatayA bhinnapadatvAshrayeNa vyAchakShate | tattu 'AnandIbhavati sphuTam' ityanuvyAkhyAne Anandasya svabhAvasiddhatvAdbhavatIti kathamityataH - sphuTamityuktamiti sudhAviruddham | anayA AnandIbhavatItyaikapadyapratIteH | sa jIvo 'nirAtaN^ko' nirbhayassan nityo.avatiShThate muktAviti shrutyarthaH | 'anAnandAdirUpatvam' AnandAdirUpatvAbhAvaH shrutau pratIyata iti | karaNe adhikaraNatvopachAraH | parvaM j~nAnasya prathamaM grahaNAt tatra tadviruddhasyaiva grahaNe kartavye shrutyanusArAdanAnandetyuktam | pUrvatrApyayameva hetuH |
(2) na jIvo j~nAnAdirUpaH, tathAshruterAnandAdirUpatvasya ananubhavAchcheti prApte siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti|| bAlasyeti| strIpuMsarUpachetanasyetyarthaH | sAmAnyoktyA sautrAdishabdaH strItvA
rthakatayA vyAkhyAtaH| sadeveti | bAlye vidyamAnamevetyarthaH | na tu pUrvam asadityevArthaH | 'puMstvam' apatyotpAdanashaktiH | strItvasyApyupalakShaNametat | 'yauvane' yauvanAvasthAyAm | anena puMstvAdivaditi dR^iShTAntAMsho vyAkhyAtaH | sUtre avadhAraNArthakatushabdasya satastviti sambandham, asyetyasya prakR^itatadguNasAratvapraviShTaguNaparAmarshakatvamabhipratya svarUpatayA mukteH pUrvamapi satAmeva AnandAdInAmityuktam | yadyapi sUtrAnusArAtsata eva AnandAderiti vaktumuchitam | tathApi j~nAnAnandAderojobalAderbahudharmasya saN^grahAya bahuvachanaprayogaH | 'vyaktyapekShayaiva' muktau samyagabhivyaktinamittenaiva, na tUtpattinimittenetyevakArArthaH | samyagvyaktavyapekShayetyanena yogashabdo nimittArthaH, ambuvadagrahaNAdityatreva tushabdo visheShArtho.apItyuktaM bhavati| taduktiriti| AnandIbhavatItyAdivyapadesha ityarthaH | upapadyate yata iti sheShaH| anena sUtre tadvyapadeshasyeti vipariNatapadasya anuShaN^gaH, yogAdityasya AvR^ittishcha sUchitA| asya hetoH na 'doShaH' na shrutivirodhAkhyo doSha iti pUrvasUtrAdanuShaktasAdhyenAnvayaH | anena - 'puMstvAdivat' yathA puruShayoShidAdInAmapatyotpAdanashakteH svarUpatve.api yauvane abhivyakteH anyadA anabhivyakteshcha idAnIM pumAn pUrvaM tu neti vyavahAravisheShopayogitA, tathA j~nasya jIvasya mukteH pUrvamapi sato.asya j~nAnAnandAdigaNasamudAyasya muktau 'sataH' prasannAdIshvarAttatprasAdena samyagabhivyaktirUpayogAnnimittAdeva AnandIbhavatItyAdivyapadeshasya pUrvamAnandAdyananubhavasya mumukShuprayatnasya cha yogAdupapatterna doSho na shrutyAdivirodhaH| ato bhavatyeva jIva AnandAdirUpa iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(3) nanu prAgasatAmutpattivAdinI shrutiH kiM na syAt, kimabhivyaktikalpanayetyata Aha - balamiti || 'ojaH' parAkramaH | 'sahaH' sahanashaktiH | 'anAkulam' asaMshayaviparyayaM j~nAnam | etAni jIvasya svarUpANyeva muktau 'paramAdvibhoH' viShNoH tatprasAdAt mahattayA vyajyanta eva, na tu prAgasanti apUrvatayA utpadyanta ityarthaH | ata eva bR^ihadbhAShye -
alpaM tejastathaivAlpaM jIvarUpaM hi saMsR^itau |
tathaiva sumahattejaH karoti bhagavAn mahat || iti ||
svarUpasyaiva tejaso mokShe bhagavataH samyagvyaktirevoktA na tUtpattiH | 'alpaM tejaH sumahatkaroti' alparUpaM parimANato mahatkaroti muktAvityarthaH | etachcha sajjIvaviShayam | evaM tamoyogyAnAM duHkhAdirUpatvaM nitya
saMsAriNAM mishratvaM cha j~nAtavyamiti | gaupavanashrutiriti | yata iti sheShaH | asyAtaH satAM vyaktimeva AnandIbhavatItyAdishrutirAha na tUtpattimityadhyAhR^itasAdhyenAnvayaH | 
(4) yaduktaM jIvasvarUpabhUtAnAmAnandAdInAM prAganabhivyaktAnAM mokShe abhivyaktiriti tadayuktam | jIvasvarUpasya nityAbhivyaktatvena tatsvarUpabhUtAnAmIshvaraprasAdena abhivyaktyayogAditi chet - tatra praShTavyam, kiM jIvasyAnandAdirUpatvamaN^gIkR^itya tadAvaraNAbhAvAttannivR^ittirnAbhyupagamyate?  kiM vA AnandAdirUpatvamevAnaN^gIkR^ityedamuchyate? prathamapakShadUShaNAya (na cha jIvasvarUpasyApyAnandAdeH AvaraNanimittAtprAganabhivyaktiH, IshvaraprasAdena AvaraNanivR^ittau tadabhivyaktirbhavatIti tannivR^ittyarthAtyarthaprasAdArthaM mumukShuprayatno yukta iti vAchyam| AvaraNAbhAvena tannivR^itteranabhyupagamAdityAshaN^kAM parihartuM) sUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - nityeti|| sautrAnyathAshabdArthamAha - vyaktyanaN^gIkara iti | jIvasya AnandAdirUpatvamaN^gIkR^ityaAvaraNAbhAvAnmokShe AvaraNanivR^ittirUpavyakteranaN^gIkAre AvaraNasyaivAnaN^gIpashchAdvyaktirityanaN^gIkAra ityanyathAshabdArtha uktaH| tasyApyayamevAshayaH| idaM chApAdyatraye.apyanveti| 'devAnAM' muktiyogyAnAmiti | anena sUtre j~nAnAmityasyAnuvR^ittissUchitA | trividhAdhikArinirdeshena vAshabdo vyavasthitavikalpArtha iti sUchitam| asyetyanuvR^ittapadavyAkhyAnam - AnandAdInAmiti sarvatrAnveti | uttaratra AnandAdirvaiShayiko grAhyaH | prasajyete ityetadvipariNAmena pUrvatrApi sambadhyate | tathA cha vyaktyanaN^gIkAre devAnAmAnandAdInAM devasambandhyAnandaj~nAnAdInAM 'nityopalabdhiH' nityamanubhavaH prasajyate | evaM vyaktyanaN^gIkAre 'asurANAM' mokShayogyAnAmAnandAdInAm 'anupalabdhiH' AnandAdyupalabdhiviruddhaduHkhAdyupalabdhiH nityaM svarUpaduHkhopalabdhireva prasajyate, na tu kadAchidviShayasukhAdyanubhavaH | evaM vyaktyanaN^gIkAre 'manuShyANAM' madhyamAnAm AnandAdInAM nityopalabdhyanupalabdhI prasajyete iti yojanA| nityopalabdhyanupalabdhI ityanena anyatarashabdaH ubhayArthatayA vyAkhyAtaH | chaH samuchchaye | atrAnupalabdhishabdena kevalAyAH duHkhAdyanapalabdhivishiShTAyAH sukhAdyupalabdherabhAvo vivakShitaH | tathA cha sukhAdyanupalabdhyApAdanena duHkhAdyanupalabdhireva ApAditA bhavati| evaM cha madhyamamanuShyANAM mishrarUpatvAtsvarUpabhUtasya sukhasya duHkhasya chopalabdhiH samaiva syAt, na tu kadAchidviShayasukhaduHkhopalabdhiH, AvaraNAbhAve anubhavAbhAvAyogAditi bhAvaH | anena asurapakShe anupalabdhyApAdanamayuktam, teShAM svarUpAnandAderabhAvAdeva anupalabdhyupapatteH| anAvaraNasya avidyamAnAnandAnupalabdhiM pratyaprayojakatvAditi shaN^kA, evaM bhAvaM pratyaprayojakatvAditishaN^kA cha nirastA | asurapakShe sUtre anupalabdhipadena AsurAvidyetyAdAviva prakR^itasukhAdyupalabdhiviruddhaduHkhAdyupalabdhereva vivakShitatvAt| madhya
mamanuShyapakShe.apyanupalabdhipadena niravadhAraNAyA duHkhAdyupalabdhereva vivakShitatvAt | ata eva TIkAyAmetachcha sajjIvaviShayam, keShAJNchidduHkhAdirUpatvaM mishratvaM cha j~nAtavyamityuktam| atra kechit - 'nityAnandaH' ityAdipramANAnusAreNa anyatarashabdasvArasyAchcha devAnAmityAdibhAShyaM sautrakramamullaN^ghya 'anyataraniyamaH' ityasya vyAkhyAnarUpaM 'nityopalabdhya- nupalabdhI' ityetannityopalabdhyanupalabdhiprasaN^ga ityasya vyAkhyAnarUpaM, sUtre uktilAghavAya madhyamajIvAnAM prathamamApAdanam | evamasurapakShe anupalabdhirupalabdhyabhAva eva, na tu duHkhopalabdhiH, sA tu sAkShAdApAdyA, paramparayA tu sukhopalabdherabhAva iti vyAchakShate| tanna - 'nityAnandaH' iti pramANasyoktapakSha evAnuguNatvAt, vakShyamANarItyA anyatarashabdasyobhayaparatva eva svArasyAchcha, bhAShyaTIkAtattvapradIpAnanuguNatvAchcha| bhAShyaTIkayordevadAnavamishrakrameNApAdanAt| tattvapradIpe.api vyaktyanaN^gIkAre muktiyogyA vinaiva sAdhanasampattyAnityavyaktAnandA bhaveyuH, tamoyogyAH saMsR^itAvapi sukhaleshahInAH nityuduHkhinaH syurityAdinA devAdikrameNaivAsurapakShe duHkhopalabdhereva cha ApAdanAt |
(5) dvitIyapakShaM pramANavirodhena nirAchaShTe - (nanu yadi jIvAnAM AnandAdirUpatvaM syAttadA tasya saMsR^itau anabhivyaktyarthaM j~nAnAbhAvAtiriktAvidyAvaraNaM bhagavatprasAdena tannivR^ittishcha aN^gIkAryA syAttadeva nAsti | tadanaN^gIkAre doShAbhAvAdityAshaN^kAM pramANavirodhena nirAchaShTe) nityeti || 'nityAnandaH' yathArthaj~nAnAdirUpaH paramAtmetyarthaH| paramAtmetyanantaram evaM surA ityadhyAhAro.abhipretaH| ata eva smR^itau 'nityAnandaj~nAnabalA devAH' ityuktam| tattvapradIpe tu paramAtmano nityAnandatvoktyA devAnAM cha nityAnandatvaM vivakShitam, devabhAgatvAttasyetyuktam | tasyAbhiprAyastu atra paramAtmashabdena uttamajIvarAshirvivakShita iti sudhAyAmuktam | chandrikAyAmapi tathaivoktam | 'asurAH' tamoyAgyAH 'naivaM' muktiyogyavanna, kintu tadviruddhaduHkhamithyAj~nAnasvarUpA ityarthaH | 'manuShyAH' madhyamAstu 'evam' AnandAdirUpAH 'anevaM' duHkharUpAshchetyarthaH | iti hIti | hishabdaH prasiddhau | shrutirityanantaraM jIvasya AnandAdirUpatvaM vaktIti vAkyasheShaH | tathA cha jIvasyAnandAdirUpatvAnaN^gIkAre shrutivirodhApatteH tasya tadaN^gIkAryamiti bhAvaH | yadyapyatrArthe 'vij~nAnAtmA' iti prAgudAhR^itashrutiratideShTuM yuktA | 'balamAnanda ojaH' iti shrutirvodAhartuM yuktA | tathApi trividhasyApi jIvasvarUpasyAnukteH shrutyantarodAharaNam |
(6) adhikaraNArthe smR^itiM chAha - bhaviShyaditi || shrutisamuchchaye chashabdaH | nityatvamAnandAdervisheShaNam | devAH muktiyogyAH 'dAnavAH' tamoyogyAH 'evaM' devavanna, kiM tarhItyata Aha - duHkhopalabdhIti | 'te' dAnavAH 'duHkhopalabdhimAtrA' duHkhAnubhavamAtrayogyA ityarthaH | yogyatvaM tu saMsR^itAvapyasti | mAtrasha
bdena sukhopalabdhirvyAvartyate | madhyamamAnuShAstu 'ubhayAtmakAH' sukhaduHkhamishrasvarUpAH |
(7) nanu devAnAM sukhaj~nAnAdirUpatvamanupapannam, saMsAre duHkhasyApyanubhavAt viparItaj~nAnasyApi darshanAchcha | evaM daityAnAM duHkhopalabdhimAtratvamapyanupapannam, saMsAre sukhasyApyanubhavAt | evaM manuShyANAM mishratvamapyayuktam, saMsAre kevalasukhaduHkhayorapyanubhavAdityata Aha - teShAmiti || upAdhirbAhyaH | tathA cha 'teShAM' devAnAM yatsvarUpAt 'anyathA' anyat 'dR^ishyaM' duHkhAdi 'tadupAdhikR^itam' jIvasvarUpopAdhyatiriktabAhyadehanimittam | upAdhinivR^ittiH kuta ityata Aha - vij~nAneti | yataH 'Atmayogyena' svayogyena 'vij~nAnena' visheShaj~nAnena tR^itIyArthe saptamI | AvirbhUtasvasvarUpeNa vyavasthitirbhavatItyarthaH | vij~nAnenAtmayogyenetyAdinA nityasaMsAriNAmapyAvaraNAbhAve aniShTaprasaN^goktyA cha teShAmapi AvaraNanivR^ittyA svarUpAvirbhAvo.astIti sUchitam | 
(8) kiM tannijarUpamityata uktaM vivR^iNoti - samyagiti | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | 'devAnAM' muktiyogyAnAM samyagj~nAnameveti | 'vimishritaM' viparItamiti atra j~nAnamityanuShajyate | daityAnAM tvityanvitastushabdo visheShArthaH | 'j~nAnasya' svarUpaj~nAnasya 'evam' uktaprakAreNa 'vyavasthitiH' sthitirityarthaH | itishabdasya bhaviShyatparvaNIti pUrveNAnvayaH | adhikaraNArtha ukta iti sheShaH |
|| iti puMstvAdhikaraNam || 16 ||
|| 17. kartR^itvAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvakartR^itvaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate| shrutivirodhaM saMshayabIjaM darshayati - Ishvarasyeti| 'nAnyaH kartA' ityAdishrutAvanyaniShedhAdIshvarasyaiva kartR^itvamuktamityarthaH | itIti | iti shrutAvityarthaH | 'jIvasya' jIvasyApi 'upalabhyate' pratIyate | kartR^itvamityanuShaN^gaH | yAdR^ishaM karma kurute jIvaH tAdR^ikkarmaphalam 'abhi- sampadyate' prApnotIti vajasaneyashrutyarthaH | shruteH jIvaikaniShThatvaj~nApanAya taditi phalavAkyasheShodAharaNam | Ishravasyaiveti sAvadhAraNayA saMshayabIjoktyA svAtantryeNa pAratantryeNa vA kenApi rUpeNa na jIvaH kartA, kiM tvIshvara eveti pUrvapakSho jIvakartR^itvAbhAvasya shrutatvAditi yuktishcha sUchitA | yojanA tu na jIvaH kartA yataH shrutAvIshvarasyaiva kartR^itvamuktaM na chAnyatrApi 'yat' iti shrutirastIti vAchyam | yat Ishvarasyaiva kartR^itvamuktam itaravyapadeshAdityAdAvananyayogena samarthitam | tathA cha phalavachChrutyapekShayA sayuktikashruteH prAbalyAt anayA anyasyA bAdha iti bhAva iti |
