(2) evaM prApte siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || kartR^itvAbhAva iti | kartR^itvasAmAnyAbhAva ityarthaH | shAstrasyeti | 'yajeta svargakAmaH' 'brAhmaNo na hantavyaH' ityAdividhiniShedharUpashAstrasyetyarthaH | aprayojakatveti | prayujyate.anena puruShaH shAstre iti vyutpattyA prayojakaM prayojanaM tato bahuvrIhiH, tathA cha vaiyarthyaprasaN^gAdityarthaH | na hi kartAramantareNAraNyarodanAyamAnashAstrasya sArthakyaM bhavatIti bhAvaH | anena jIvasya kartR^itvAN^gIkAra eva 'shAstrArthavattvAt' shAstrasyArthavattvasiddheH anyathA.asiddheriti hetvaMsho vipakShe hetUchChittirUpabAdhakoktimukhena vyAkhyAtaH | anuvR^ittasya j~na ityasyArtho jIvo.apIti | 'kartA' kartaiva na tvakartA.aN^gIkArya iti sheShaH | apItyanena sUtre.apyarthakachashabdasyAnavR^ittiH sUchitA |
(3) nanu jIvasya svataH kartR^itvAbhAve.api paragatakartR^itve svIyatvAgraho.astyeva ataH kAlpanikakartR^itvavantaM jIvaM prati vidhiniShedhashAstraM pravartatAmityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - vihAreti | jIvaH kartetyanuShajyate| tattvata iti sheShaH| anena sUtre.apyanuvR^ittisheShau sUchitau| apishabdo visheShaNasamuchchayArthaH| AdishabdAt 'so.a- shnute sarvAn' (tai.2.1.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | tathA cha 'api' vigalitAkhilakalpane.api mokShe 'strIbhirvA' ityAdinA vihArapadoktasaJNcharaNakrIDAkAmyaprAptyAdikartR^itvokteH| 'tattvataH' paramArthata eva jIvaH kartA na kalpanayeti yojanA | asya mokShaprakaraNatvaM tu ChAndogye taittirIye cha 'paraM jyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate' (ChAM.8.3.4.) 'brahmAvidApnoti param' (tai.2.1.) iti cha mokShaM prastutyAmnAtatvAt j~nAyate | shrutistu daharanaye vyAkhyAtA |
(4) nanvastu mokShe jIvasya svAbhAvikaM kartR^itvaM prAmANikatvAt | saMsAre tu kAlpanikameva kiM na syAt | tAvatA shAstrasArthakyAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - upAdAnAditi || sAdhaneti | mokShasvargAdyarthaM vedavichArayAgAdirUpetyarthaH | Adishabdena taditikartavyatA gR^ihyate | yadvA - tattvapradIparItyA ChedAdyarthakuThArAdikaM sAdhanapadoktam Adipadena kAShThAdirUpaviShaya ukta iti dhyeyam | upAdAnam anuShThAnaM sampAdanamiti yAvat | tasya pratIteH pratyakShasiddhatvAjjIvasyetyarthaH | tatashcha phaladarshanAditi chashabdArthaH | asyApi jIvo.api karteti pUrvasAdhyenAnvayaH | yadvA - tattvapradIpe na kevalaM shAstrArthavatvAjjIvasya kartR^itvaM pratipadyAmahe, api tu pratyakShata eva tatsiddhamityAhetyavatArya chashabdAnna cha tadbAdho dR^ishyata ityuktahetusamuchchayArthatvasyoktatvAt TIkAkArasyApyayameva chashabdArtho.abhipretaH | ata evottaraTIkAyAmevamupapattyA pratyakSheNa chetyuktam | chashabdaprayogena sUtre.api chashabdo.anuShaJNjanIya iti sUchitam | kechittu - atra sUtre pUrvasUtre cha krameNa shaN^kAdvayaparihArAt na chashabdaH, mauktAkAlpanikatvasAMsArikAkAlpanikatvarUpaviShayabhedAt | tathApi avAntarasAdhyabhede.api akAlpanikatvasAmAnyasya pUrvasUtre yuktyA atra tu pratyakSheNa chopAdAnAt bhAShye chashabdaH prayukta ityAhuH | tattu uttaraTIkAtattvapradIpaviruddham | tatra kartR^itvasyaiveha sAdhyatvenokteH |
(5) evaM saMsAre shAstrArthavattvarUpayuktyA sAdhanAdyupAdAnapratyakSheNa cha sAdhitaM jIvakartR^itvaM shrutyA.api samarthayatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - vyapadeshAchcheti || itIti | upAsanAkhyakriyAyAm upAsItetyAtmanaH kartR^itvokteratyarityarthaH | asya hetorjIvo.api karteti pUrvasAdhyenAnvayaH na kevalaM yuktipratyakShAbhyAM, kintu shruteshcheti chashabdArthaH | tathA choktaM bhAratatAtparyanirNaye -
pratyakShaiShA kartR^itA jIvasaMsthA |
tathA.a.agamAdanumAnAchcha sarvam || ityAdi ||
'lokaM' sarvAshrayaM prakAshamAnaM vA 'AtmAnaM' viShNumupAsIta jIva iti bR^ihadAraNyakaChandogashrutyarthaH |
(6)à¤¼ nanu atra jIva upAsItetyuktyabhAvAt kathamayaM jIvasya kartR^itvavyapadeshassyAdityatastadupapAdanAya vipakShe bAdhakoktiparaM na chedityaMshaM vyAchaShTe - anyatheti | jIvasya upAsanAkriyAnAM kartR^itvena shrutyanabhimatatve kriyAyA akartR^ikatvajaDakartR^ikatvayorasambhavAchChrutivaiyarthyApattyA tatparihArAya paramAtmana eva kriyAkartR^itvena tadabhimatatve chetyarthaH| Atmaivetyanena nirdeshaviparyayapada tadvinyAsavyatyAsaparamiti sUchitam| asmin pakShe AtmA paramAtmaiva svAtmAnamanyaM vA lokamupAsIteti shrutyarthaprApteriti karmatvenetyasya kevalakarmatvenetyartho.avagantavyaH| anyamiti pakShe tu yathA sheShoktiH| tathA chAsya kartR^itvAnnAsti chAsau viparItanirdeshaH tasmAnna jIvo.akartA kiM tu kartaiveti viparyayaparyavasAne jIvasyApi kartR^itAsiddhiriti bhAvaH| na cha jIvaparayorubhayorapi kartR^itve gauravaM doShaH, prAmANikatvAt |
(7) nanvevaM jIvasyApikartR^itve  kathamitaravyapadeshAdityAdau Ishvarasyaiva kartR^itvaM samarthitam | kathaM cha nAnyaH kartA iti shrutirupapadyate | atastadvirodho.astyevetyAshaN^kya tatparihArAya sUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - tarhIti || jIvasyApi kartR^itva ityarthaH | uktamiti nAnyaH kartA iti shrutAviti sheShaH | yadvA - itaravyapadeshAdityAdau kathaM samarthitamityarthaH | yathA j~nAne ityanena sUtre saptamyantAdvitiriti sUchitam | j~nAsyAmItyanantaraM ichChata iti sheShaH | karmaNItyanena kriyAyAmityasya jIvasyetyanena j~nasyeti vipariNatapadasya cha anuvR^ittissUchitA | jIvasyetyanantaram anuShaktAniyamapadaM niyamasyApyupalakShakam | dR^iShTAntasamuchchaye visheShaNasamuchchaye vA.apishabdaH | tathA chAhabhidaM surUpaM sugandhaM susvaraM vA j~nAsyAmi, viparItaM na pashyAmi na jighrAmi na shrR^iNvAnItyevaM spR^ihayato jIvasya yathopalabdhau j~nAne aniyamaH svechChAnusAreNa na j~nAnalAbhaH 
pratIyate | evaM tathA kriyAyAM karmaNyapi kariShyAmIti saN^kalpite.api vyApAre aniyamaH pratyetavyaH | taddR^iShTAntenAtrAniyamaH sAdhyA iti yAvat | Ishvarasya tu j~nAne karmaNi cha niyama iti yojanA | tathA cha yata evaM jIvasya karmaNi niyamAbhAvaH, Ishvarasya tu tadbhAvassiddho.ato.ananyAdhInakartR^itvavivakShayA Ishvarasyaiva kartR^itvaM na jIvasyetyuktaM prAk | na tu sarvathA kartR^itvAbhAveneti na pUrvoktavirodha iti bhAvaH | j~nAsyAmIti ichChata ityanena cha dR^iShTAntaH sAdhyavikala iti shaN^kA parihR^itA | kathamiti chet - na hi jij~nAsurj~nAne sAkShAdvyApriyate, yena niyamena j~nAnaprAptiH, kiM tu j~nAnakriyAsAdhana eva, na tu phalechChayA sAdhanAnuShThAne phalAvyabhichAro.adR^iShTa iti TIkoktarItyeti gR^ihANa |
(8) Ishvarasyaiva niyamanakartR^itvaM, na jIvasyetyatra pramANamAha - ya iti || iti cha shrutiriti | iti shrutirapyevamevAha, na kevalaM sUtramiti chArthaH | yaH chaturmukhAdijIvaM tattadantargato niyamayati eSha paramAtmA tavAntaryAmIti vAjasaneyashrutyarthaH | atreshvarasya jIvaniyAmakatvoktyA tatpreraNAM vinA jIvAnAM niyamena kartR^itvAbhAvaH svechChAnusArikartR^itvAbhAvaH, Ishvarasya tu niyAmakatvAt tadbhAvo.avagamyate |
(9) nanUbhayoH kartR^itvAvisheShe.api Ishvarasyaiva niyamena kartR^itvaM, na jIvasyetyetadvailakShaNyaM kiM nimittamiti pR^ichChati -kuta iti || niyamAniyamau IshajIvayoH kutaH kiMnimittakAvityarthaH | atra svAtantryapAratantryanimittau niyamAniyamAviti parihAraM vaktum IshajIvayoH svAtantryapAratantrye sAdhayatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - shaktIti || alpashaktitvAdityanena mukhyatvAchChaktishabdaH pUrNashaktiparaH viparyayashabdastu tadviparItAlpashaktipara iti sUchitam | j~nasyetyanuvR^ittapadasyArtho jIvasyeti | upalakShaNametat | Ishvarasya pUrNashaktitvAdityapi draShTavyam | asvAtantryaM svAtantryamiti vakShyamANamatrApi sambadhyate |
(10) yuktyantareNeshajIvayoH svAtantryapAratantrye samarthayatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - samAdhyabhAvAchcheti || samAdhAnamalaMbuddhirapUrNakAmatvamiti yAvat | na kevalamalpashaktitvAditi chArthaH | jIvasyeti vartate | sUtre tu j~nasyeti vartate upalakShaNametat | samAdhibhAvAchcheshvarasya svAtantryamityapi draShTavyam | chashabda uktAnuktahetusamuchchAyakaH | astUktahetubhyaH IshajIvayoH svAtantryapAratantryasiddhiH | tAvatA niyamAniyamayoH kiMnimittakatvamuktaM bhavatItyata Aha - ata iti | niyamAniyamAviti sheShaH | tathA cha yata evamIshajIvayoH svAtantryapAratantrye pratIyete atastayostAbhyAM nimittAbhyAM karmaNi niyamAniyamau pratipattvyAvityarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu ata ityasya 'yathA cha takShobhayathA' iti sUtreNAnvayamabhipretya ato.asvAtantryapramANebhyaH kartR^itvamAnebhyashcha yathA cha takShobhayathA vyapadishyate evaM jIvo.asvatantraH kartA cheti vyapadishyata ityuktam |
(11) nanu yadi jIvasya na svAtantryeNa kartR^itvam, api tu IshvarechChayaiva, tarhi kathaM jIvaH kartochyate, svatantraH khalu kartetyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - yatheti || yathA cha 'takShNo' vardhakeH prAsAdakArayitR^irAjAdipreritatvaM tatkartR^itvaM cha asti, evaM jIvasyApi IshvaraniyatatvaM ghaTAdikartR^itvaM chAstvityadhyAhAreNa yojanA | kArayitR^iniyatatvaM kartR^itvamityanenobhayathetyuktaprakAradvayaM darshitam | evaM jIvasyApItyanena chashabdasya dArShTAntikasamuchchayArthatvamabhipraiti | kechittu - sUtre ubhayathA cheti chashabdasambandhamabhipretya bhAShye kartR^itvaM chetyuktamityAhuH | tanna, tadbhAShyasyobhayathetyuktaprakAradvayasamuchchayaparatvena chashabdArthapradarshakatvAbhAvAt | tathA cheshvarAdhIne.api jIve dR^iShTAntabalAtkArakAprayojyatvarUpAmukhyasvAtantryagarbhitakartR^itvavyapadesho yujyata eveti bhAvaH |
(12) nanu kiM takShNa iva jIvasya kartR^itvashaktirjIvAdhInaiva, IshvarAdhInatvaM tu vachanavetanadAnAdivat | uta kartR^itvashaktirapIshvarAdhInA | yadyAdyaH tarhIshvarasyaiva kartR^itvamiti gataH pakShaH | dvitIye na jIvasya kartR^itvashaktirityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - parAditi || seti prakR^itatvopapAdakaM, yA shaktisUtre prakR^itA, yA cha takShakadR^iShTAntena upapAditetyarthaH | cho.apyarthaH | kartR^itvetyataH prAk jIvasyetyupaskAryam | shaktirityanena taditi bhinnapadasyArtha uktaH | sAmarthyamiti vaktavye shaktiriti tachChabdaparyAyashabdenArthakathanam | shaktisUtragatashaktishabdavivakShayeti dhyeyam | kechittu - sUtre shaktiriti sheShaH | tachChruterityekaM padaM, tathA cha IshAdhInatvena shruteriti tadartha ityAhuH | 'parAdeva' paramAtmanaH sAkashAdAgataiva tadadhInaiva na jIvAdhInetyarthaH | anena sautratushabdo.avadhAraNArthatayA vyAkhyAtaH | tasmAnnApasiddhAnta iti vAkyasheShaH |
(13) kuta ityatastatra hetutvena shruterityetadyojayati - kartR^itvamiti || kartR^itvakaraNatvapadAbhyAM tachChaktirupalakShyate| tatrAdyaM jIvasya dvitIyamindriyAdeH | 'svabhAvaH' prakR^ityAdInAM pariNAmAdiH | alpaj~natvAlpashaktitvAdirUpo vA| 'chetanA' chetaso vyAptiH 'bahusmaraNashaktistu chetanetyabhidhIyate' ityukteshchaitanyaM vA| 'dhR^itiH' dehAdidhAraNasAmarthyam| Ahatya 'ime' bhAvAH 'yatprasAdAt' yasya paramAtmano.anugrahAdichChayA santi 'yadupekShayA' yatkaTAkShAbhAve na santi ityarthaH| aneneshvarasya kartumakartumanyathA kartuM chAsti sAmarthyam, saN^kalpAbhAvAt tathA na karotItyuktaM bhavati| asya yachChabdasya tatra prakR^itena tachChabdenAnvayaH | 'hi' yataH shrutirityasya parAdeveti sAdhyenAnvayaH | 
(14) nanvasmin pakShe.api doSha uktaH, yadi kartR^itvashakatirIshvarAdhInA tarhi tasyaiva kartR^itvam, na jIvasya dArupratimAvadanyAdhInasyeti punashshAstravaiyarthyamityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - kR^iteti || 'tataH' kartR^itvashakterIshvarAdhInatvAdapi 'shAstrasya' vidhiniShedhAtmakasya 'aprayojakatvaM' na vidyate prayojakaM prayojanaM yasya tasya bhAvo vaiyarthyaM 'nApadyate' na prasajyate | kutaH? 'tataH' tadavaiyarthyAyaiva 'tatprerakatvasya' tasyeshvarasya jIvaprerakatvasya 'kR^itaprayatnApekShatvAt' pUrvakarmaprayatnayogyatAsApekShatvAditi 
yojanA | tata ityanena vihiteti chaturthyantaM padaM vyAkhyAtam | kR^itetyAdinA kR^iteti hetusamarpakashabdo vyAkhyAtaH | tatprerakatvasyetyanena sUtre pUrvasUtrAtpara iti vipariNatapadasya dvitIyAntaj~nashabdasya chAnuvR^ittiH prerayatItyadhyAhAraH sUchitaH | sUtre tushabd.avadhAraNe.apyarthe chetyabhipretyAdishabdArthamAha - Adishabdeneti | 'avaiShamyAdi' saN^gR^ihItamiti sheShaH | atrAdishabdenAnairghR^iNyaM gR^ihyate | anena - na tato.api jIvashakterIshvarAdhInatvAdapi shAstrasya vaiyarthyamApadyate | kutaH? yato.ayaM paramAtmA 'vihitapratiShedhA- vaiyarthyAdibhyastu' vidhiniShedhashAstrAvaiyarthyAyaiva, na tu svasya sahAyArthaM tathA svasya vaiShamyanairghR^iNyaparihArAya cha 'kR^ita- prayatnApekShastu' jIvasyAnAdikarmaprayatnasApekSha eva jIvaM bhoge prerayati, tadyogyatAmapekShya tu karmaNi, na tu tadanapekSha iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | ata evoktaM bhAratatAtparyanirNaye - 
etAnapekShyaiva phalaM dadAnI-
tyasyaiva saN^kalpa iti svatantratA || iti ||
atrAyaM chandrikokto bhAvaH - jIvasya vidhivAkyatadarthaj~nAne tajjanyasAdhanaphalechChayoH sAdhanaviShayakakR^itau cha bhagavatpreryatve.api na vidhiviShayatvakarmaphalabhAktvayoranupapattiriti na shAstrapravR^ittivaiyarthyam | rAjabhaTAdyutpAditechChAdimato.api trivarNAderviShTigR^ihItasya cha sandhyopAsanAdau bhAravahanAdau cha vidhyAdidarshanena tadvadevAsvatantrakartR^itAmAtreNa tayorupapatteriti | uktaM hi gItAbhAShye - akartR^itve.api vidhidvArA IshaprasAdAdichChotpattyoktakAraNaiH karmadvArA mokSho bhavatIti na pravR^ittividhivaiyarthyamiti | vivR^itaM chaitatprameyadIpe - jIvasyAparAdhInakartR^itvAbhAve.api svasambandhitayA vidhij~nAnasyeshvaraprasAdAyattayoH karmaphalaM choddishyechChAprayatnayoradhiShThAnAdikarmakAraNasannidhAnasyakarmasambandhasya tatphalabhAktvasya cha vidhiviShayatAprayojakasya sattvAttasya vidhiviShayatvaM kintu saMsArijIvasyeti choktam | yadyapi vaiShamyAdiparihAraH pUrvameva vaiShamyasUtre kR^itaH | tathApi sa eva kartR^itvashakterIshvarAdhInatvaprayuktavaiShamyAdishaN^kAparihArAyehAdishabdena smArayituM punarukta iti na paunaruktyam |
(15) sUtrArthe smR^itimAha - pUrveti || 'saMskAro' yogyatA | chashabdau parasparasamuchchaye | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | 'sarvaM' puNyapApAdikarma jIvena kArayati tatkAraNAya taM prerayatItyarthaH | yadvA - kArayati bhojayatItyarthadvayamapi vihitakAriNaM puNyaM bhojayati kArayati cha puNyaM, niShiddhakAriNaM duHkhaM bhojayati punaH pApaM kArayati cheti tattvapradIpoktam | nanvIshvarasya jIvakarmApekShayA prerakatve tasya tatkarmAkartR^ikatvaM syAdityata Aha - tachcheti | apekShyaM cha karmetyarthaH | svayaM sAkShAttarhi tatpreraNe IshvarasyApekShyakarmAbhAva ityata Aha - anAditvAditi | karmaNaH kAryakAraNIbhUtakarmaparamparAyAstvanAditvAnnApekShyAbhAvakR^itavaiShamyAdidoSha ityarthaH | tarhi kAryakAraNarUpANAM pUrvapUrvakarmaNAmanantatvAtkathaM tatkArayitR^itvamIshvarasyopapa
dyata ityata Aha - pUrNeti | tathA cha hareramitashaktitvAdanantakarmakArayitR^itvaM tasya sambhavatyeveti na doSha iti bhAvaH | bhaviShyatparvaNi 'kR^ita' iti sUtrArtha ukta iti sheShaH|
(16) adhikaraNArthe smR^itiM chAha - etaditi || yataH 'etat' jIvasya kartR^itvam 'evaM' prAmANikam IshvaravatsvAtantryeNa chaitadevaM na, ata etatkartR^itvamasvAtantryeNAsti svAtantryavivakShayA nAstIti 'nAnyaH kartA' iti shrutAvuchyate ata ityarthaH | itIti | evaMrUpamokShadharmavachane.adhikaraNArtha ukta ityarthaH |
|| iti kartR^itvAdhikaraNam || 17 ||
|| 18. aMshAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvaviShaye shrutivirodhaH parihriyate | tatra jIvasyeshvarAMshatvamanaMshatvaM vetyanirNayapUrvapakShamabhipretya viruddhashrutidvayarUpamanirNayakAraNaM darshayati - aMshA eva hIti || 'ime' pramitA jIvAH aMshA eva pitAputrAdisambandhaiH kevalaM tadupajIvyatvena tachCheShabhUtA evetyarthaH | yadvA - tato nyUnatve sati kiJNchittatsadR^ishatvarUpAMshatvopetA ityarthaH | na tu niruktAMshatvarahitA ityevashabdArthaH | evetyanenAMshatvAnaMshatvayorvikalpo.api nirastaH | hishabdau ubhayatra prasiddhidyotakau | nanu jIvAnAmapyaMshatve kathaM tarhi hariraMshena jagatsR^ijatIti vyapadesha ityata Aha - svayamiti | sAkShAdaMshairaniruddhAdyaiH 'sarvaM' jagat 'kArayati' sR^ijatIryarthaH | tathA cha svarUpAMshaviShayaM tadvachanam | jIvAstu bhinnAMshA iti na teShAM tadviShayatvamiti bhAvaH | yadvA - svayaM sAkShAdbhinnAMshairviriJNchAdijIvaiH svapadAdabhraShTatvAnnirvikAratvAdvA.achalo hariH sR^iShTyAdi kArayatItyarthaH | 
(2) evamaMshatvashrutimudAhR^ityAnaMshatvashrutimudAharati - naiveti || siddhAntarItyA.ayaM shrutyarthaH - jIvaH 'parasya' paramAtmana aMsho na bhavati, kintvanaMsha eva | anena vikalpo nirastaH | kuta ityata Aha - na sambandha iti | yato lokapitR^ivatpoShayitR^itvAdirUpasambandharahito.ata ityarthaH | nanu pitR^itvAdirUpasambandhAbhAve.api upakartR^itvAdirUpasambandhaH kiM na syAdityato na sambandha ityetadvivR^iNoti - nApekShya iti | jIvaH parasya 'apekShyaH' upakartA.api na bhavatItyarthaH | nanvatra parashabdo neshvaraparaH, kintu jIvAntarapara ityAshaN^kAM vAkyasheShodAharaNena pariharati - tathA.apIti | yadyapyevaM, tathA.apIshvarasya jIvenAnupakR^ita
tve.api sa IshaH sarvasya jIvajAtasya 'yathAyogaM' yogyatAmanatikramya tAmapekShya svargamokShAdiphalado bhavatyeva | yogyatApekShAyAM svAtantryabhaN^ga ityata uktam - 'ekarAT' svatantra iti | tatkathamityataH - prabhuH samartha ityAha | tathA cha svAdhInayogyatApekShAyAM na svAtantryahAniriti bhAvaH | anena jIvasyAnupakartR^itvamIshvarasya tu upakartR^itvamevetyuktaM bhavati | nanvastvIshvaraH upakartA, tathApi loke svAmibhR^ityAderanyonyopakAryopakArakabhAvadarshanAttadvadIshvarasyApi kadAchit jIvopakAryatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha - na niyamya iti | 'saH' IshvaraH kenApyupakAryo na bhavatItyarthaH | anenAnaMshatvashrutiH jIva upakartavya eva, na tUpakartA, Ishvarastu upakartaiva na tUpakartavya ityabhiprAyA, bhinnAMshatvaniShedhaparA vA, evamasambandhashrutirapIshvarasya lokapitR^ivatpoShakatvAbhAvAbhiprAyA, tathA.anapekShyatvashrutirapi paramAtmanaH upakAryatvAbhAvAbhiprAyetyuktaM bhavati | pUrvapakShI tu jIvA aMshA eva, jIvo.anaMsha eveti ApAtato viruddhasAvadhAraNashrutidvayadarshanenAnirNayaM manyate | shrutAvityasyAnaMshatvaM jIvasyopalabhyate pratIyata ityanuShaktavAkyenAnvayaH |
(3) atha siddhAntayatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || yata evaM shrutidvaye viruddhoktissaMshayabIjamasti, atastatparihArArthamanyatarakoTinirNayarUpasiddhAntamAha sUtrakAra ityarthaH | sautrahetuvyAkhyAnAya nAnAvyapadeshAn darshayati - mAM rakShatviti | 'vibhuH' hariH | ahamityuktasya jIvasya spaShTaM paramAtmaputratvapratipAdakatvAdAdau smR^itimudAhR^ityAthashrutirUpavyapadeshaM darshayati - ava iti | ava ityekadeshagrahaNenAsya brahmaparatvasphorakaH 'kavIyamAnaH ka iha pravochaddevaM manaH kuto adhi prajAtam' (R^i.1.164.18.) ityuttarabhAgo.api grAhyaH | ityAdineti | evamAdivAkyena jIvasya pitR^itvaputratvAdirUpanAnAprakAreNa paramAtsambandhitvokterityarthaH | j~napadAnuvR^ittyApratij~nAvAkyaM darshayati - aMsha iti | atrAMshatvaM dvividham | upajIvakatvarUpatachCheShatvaM tannyUnatve sati tatsadR^ishatvaM cheti | ata evobhayavidhAMshatvamabhipretya sAdR^ishyaM chAMshatA.astvityanuvyAkhyAnaM chashabdAttadadhInatvaM cheti sudhA cha pravR^ittA | atrAdye aMshatve sAdhye anyathA.apItyaMshasahito nAnAvyapadeshAdityaMsho hetuH tatrAnyathetyasyopajIvyatvarAhityena vyapadeshAdityarthaH | idaM cha visheShaNaM paramAtmani vyabhichAraparihArakam | na cha pUrvatrApyanyathetyasyAnvaye j~nApakAbhAvaH | 'nAsau' ityAdinAnAvyapedashaviruddhasambandhapratipAdakAMshodAharaNasyaiva j~nApakatvAt | anyathA tadvaiyarthyApatteH | ata eva chAnyathA chetyubhayatrAnvayaj~nApakachashabdaprayogaH | na cha chashabdo vakShyamANabhedasamuchchAyaka evAstu, na sambandhasamuchchAyako.apIti vAchyam | tasyApi shabdenaiva lAbhAt | ata evAbhedenApIti bhAShye apishabdaH | na 
cha nAnAvyapadeshAkhyoktahetusamuchchAyako.apiriti vAchyam | ekenaivobhayalAbhAt | TIkAyAM sudhAyAM chAnyathetyasya vakShyamANena sambandhoktirapi vakShyamANenApi sambandhAbhiprAyikA, na tu pUrvatrAsambandhAbhiprAyikA | na cha tatsambandhitvarUpAMshatve sambandhAbhAvavyapadeshasyApi hetutve.anaMshatvashrutergatiM chAhetyuttarabhAShyavirodhaH, tatrAsambandhashruteH gatyanukteriti vAchyam | tadbhAShyasya bhedAbhedavyapadeshaprayuktAMshatvapratiyogyanaMshatvaviShayatvenAsambandharUpAnaMshatvaviShayatvAbhAvAt | ata eva asambandhashruterupakartR^itvAbhAvaviShayatvenAdyasUtrabhAShya eva gateruktatvAnna tadvirodhoM.ashatvashruterna vA paunaruktyam | dvitIye aMshatve sAdhye tUttaratrApyanvitenAnyathAchApItyaMshasahitena dAshakitavAdItyAdinokto heturyojyaH | hetvantareNaitatsamarthayata iti TIkAyAm etachChabdo.apyaMshatvasAmAnyapara iti chandrikAkArAH | bhAvabodhakArAstu atra tadadhInatve sati tatsAdR^ishyamaMshatvaM paramAtmanaH putratvaM punnAmno narakAtrANakartR^itvena jIvaniyAmakatvarUpameva | jIvasya paramAtmapitR^itvamapi tajj~nAnena tatsaMrakShyatvena tadadhInatvameva | tatra tadadhInatvarUpasambandhatvAMshe nAnAvyapadesho hetuH | tatsadR^ishatvAMshe tu anyathAchApItyAdiH hetuH | anyathA chApItyatra chashabdo vakShyamANAbhedavyapadeshasamuchchAyakaH | apishabdastu bhedAbhedavyapadeshAkhyahetornAnAvyapadesharUpapUrvoktahetunA saha samuchchayArthaH | yathA cha 'anyaH paro.anyo jIvaH' (pArAsharyA) ityaMsho.anyathAshabdoktabhadavyapadeshaH | tathA 'nAsAvasya kutashchana' 'nAyaM tasyApi kashchana' ityaMsho.api | 'asau' paramAtmA 'asya' jIvasya 'kutashchana' kenApi prakAreNopakartavyo na, kintUpakartaiva | 'ayaM' jIvo.api tasya paramAtmanaH kashchanopakartA na, kintUpakartavya eveti jIvaparamAtmanoH sadopajIvyopajIvakatvakathena bhedavyapadesha eva nAsambandhavyapadeshaH | hetvantareNaitatsamarthayata iti TIkA.apyaMshatvAntargatatadadhInatvasAdhakanAnAvyapadesharUpahetvapekShayA hetvantareNa tadantargatatsadR^ishatvAMshaM sAdhayatItyabhiprAyaketyAhuH | 'avaH pareNa' iti R^iN^mantre tR^itIyA paJNchamyarthe | jAta iti uchyata iti brahmeti cha sheShaH | adhItyasyAdhikyenetyarthaH | pretyupasargastu utpattAvatishayamAha | yadvA - adhItyasya brahmetyarthaH | kuta iti tasiH ShaShThyarthe | tathA cha yataH 'pareNa' parAddhareH 'avaH' avamaH yo jIvaH 'asya' jagataH svasya vA 'pitaraM' paramAtmAnam 'anuveda' yathAvajjAnAti | ato.ayaM 'paraH' paramAtmA 'ena' etenAnena 'avareNa' jIvena 'jAtaH' utpanna iti vyapadishyata ityarthaH | nanu tajj~nAtatvAttajjAtatvoktau devadattaj~nAte yaj~nadatte.api tajjAtatoktiH syAdityataH tajj~nAnaM durlabhamityAha - kavIyamAna iti | 'iha' loke 'kavIyamAnaH' sarvaj~nakalpaH tattvenAbhimataH ko nu ko vA iha prajAsu brahma prAvochat na ko.api | tathA 'kutaH' kasya cha 'devaM' devasambandhi parabrahmaviShayaM 'mano' j~nAnamAdhikyena samutpannam | na kasyApItyarthaH | tathA cha paramAtmaj~nAvaddevadattAdij~nAnasya durlabhatavAbhAvAnna tajj~nAtR^iShu tatpitR^itvAdivyapadeshaprasaN^ga iti bhAvaH| tattvapradIpe tu yo.avaro.asya svasya jagato vA pitaraM yathAvadveda 'pareNa' paramAtmaprasAdena, nAvarabhUtaparamAtmaprasAdeneti yAva
t| kathaM paramAtmano.a- varatvam? darshanakramamapekShya, jIvaH svasvarapadarshanAntaraM hi bhagavantaM pashyati | tathA chAnte dR^ishyamAntavAdavaratvamiti vyAkhyAtam | 'trINi padA nihitA guhAsu yastadveda sa pituShpitA sat' (mahA.1.1.4.) iti taittirIyashruterayamarthaH | yasya 'trINi padAni' svarUpANi nArAyaNavAsudevavaikuNThAkhyAnigUhitatvAt 'guhAsu' shvetadvIpAdiShu nihitAni | tadbrahma yo veda 'saH' jIvaH 'pituH' jagatpituH brahmaNaH pitA 'asat' abhavadityarthaH |
striyaH satIstAm u me puMsa AhuH pashyadakShaNvAnna vichetadandhaH |
kaviryaH putraH sa ImAchiketa yastA vijAnAtsa pituShpitA.asat ||
iti R^iN^mantrasyAyamarthaH - 'satI' satyaH nirduShTAH striyaH strIliN^gashabdavAchyAH 'me' madupAsyAH yA bhagavanmUrtayaH 'tAm u' tAneva tA eva 'puMsaH' paramapuruShAnAhuH | vedAdayo yA devatetyAdistrIliN^gashabdaiH pratipAdayanti tA eva puruShAdipulliN^gashabdairapi pratipAdayantIti bhAvaH | vidheyavivakShayA tAn puMsa iti pulliN^gaprayogaH | yo.adhikArI tAH 'pashyat' pashyati sa chakShuShmAn | yo 'na vichetat' na vijAnAti so.andhaH | yo bhagavanmUrtIH pashyati jIvaH tachchakShureva saphalaM tadanyanniShphalamavidyamAnaprAyameveti bhAvaH | 'yaH kaviH' sarvaj~no bhagavatputro.api viriJNchaH 'sa Im' sa eva 'A' samantAtsamyak 'chiketa' jAnAti | yashcha 'tAH' mUrtayo 'vijAnAt' vyajAnAt vijAnAti saH 'pituH' jagatpituH viShNorabhivyaJNjakatvAnnimittAt 'pitA' janakaH 'asat' bhavediti | ma ityasmachChabdena dIrghatamA nAma R^iShiH gR^ihyate | asya taddraShTR^itvAt | tattvapradIpe tu yAH 'satIH' nirduShTAH striyo vedAbhimAninyastAn paramapuruShAnAhuH vedAdishabdairj~nAninaH, shrutirityAdistrIliN^gashabdavAchyA evamaddR^iShTAH vedAbhimAnidevatAH veda ityAdipulliN^gashabdavAchyAnAhuriti yAvat | abhimAnivyapekShayA chAyaM vyapadeshaH | 'akShaNvAn' j~nAnadR^iShTimAneva tAn pashyati nAj~nAnI | yaH kaviH 'putro' brahmA sa eva 
yo brahmANaM vidadhAti pUrvaM
yo vai vedAMshcha prahiNoti tasmai (shve.6-18.) iti shruteH |
'tena brahma hR^idA ya Adikavaye' ityAdismR^iteshcha | 'A' samantAdveda yaH tAni ChandAMsi vishiShTatvena jAnAti sAkShAdviShNuvAchakatvena saH 'pituH' viShNoH pitA bhavati | vyaJNjakatvAchChandasAM tajj~nAtvApuruShasyeti bhAva iti vedAbhimAnidevatAparatayA vyAkhyAtam | 'dvA suparNA' ityAtharvaNashrutistu dyubhvAdhikaraNe vyAkhyAtA |
(4) yannAnAvyapadeshAdaMsho jIva iti sUtrakR^idAha, tatra shrutiM chAha - tathA cheti || chashabdo bhinnakramaH | na kevalaM sUtrakR^itaiva nAnAvyapadeshenAMshatvaM sAdhitam, kintu shrutyA.apIti chashabdArthaH | tAM shrutiM paThati - aMsha iti | hishabdaH prasiddhau | eSha iti ka ityapekShAyAmAha - ya iti | tathA cha ya utpattinAshavAnpuruShaH prasiddho.ayaM jIvaH paramAtnoM.asha iti pratij~nArthaH | chashabdo parasparasamuchchaye | kuta ityata Aha - nAneti | hi yataH 'enaM' jIvaM parasya pitetyAdinAnAprakAreNa vyapadishanti vedA ata ityarthaH | 
itishabdAH prakAravachanAH | chashabdo dvirgR^ihItaH sarvatrAnvitaH prakArANAM parasparasamuchchayamAha | itItyasya iti pArAsharyAyaNashrutiriti pUrveNAnvayaH |
(5) hetvantareNAMshatvaM samarthyate - anyatheti || tamaMshaM vyAkhyAti - anya iti | TIkAyAmanya itIti prAyikaH pAThaH | anyathetIti pAThaH sUtrAMshapratIkagrahaNarUpaH svarasaH | 'anyathA cha' vakShyamANAbhedApekShayA paramAtmabhinnatveneti yAvat | shrutirityanantaram enaM vyapadishatIti sheShaH | chashabdArthaH prAgevoktaH | iyaM cha shrutiH nAsAvityasya vaiyarthyaparihArAya bhede asambandhe cha pramANam | arthastu prAgevokteH |
(6) bhedapratiyogyabhedavyapadeshaM darshayati - brahmeti || brahmaiveme dAshA ityupasaMhArasthaM vAkyAntaraM shAkhAntarasthaM vA | yadvA - brahmaiveme dAshA ityAdipadArthaparashrutivAkyodAharaNam | atra ye dAshAH nautArakAH kaivartAH te, ye cha 'kitavAH' dyUtakR^itaH, ye chAmI 'dAsAH' svAmiShvAtmAnaM upakShipantaH te sarve.api brahmaiveti dAshakitavAdyuddeshena brahmAbhedo vidhIyata ityasyAbhedavyapadeshopapattiriti bhAvena dAshakitavAditvamityasya tAtparyArthamAha - abhedenApIti | na kevalam 'anyaH paraH' iti bhedena, kintvabhedenApItyapishabdArthaH | adhIyata ityanantaraM brahmasUtre AtharvaNikA iti sheShaH | tathA chaitachChrutidvaye jIveshayorbhedAbhedokteranyatarashrutibAdhasya chAyogAt sAkShAdbhedAbhedayoshcha virodhAdanupapatteH shrutidvayAnyathA.anupapattyA bhedamaN^gIkR^ityAbhedasthAne aMshatvaM cha vaktavyamiti bhAvaH |
(7) nAnAvyapadeshahetunAMshatvasAdhanasya yathA shrutisamAkhyoktA, tathA bhedAbhedoktyanyathA.anupapattyA.apyaMsho jIva ityatrApi shrutisamAkhyAmAha - tathA cheti || anyathetyAdinA yathA sUtrakR^idAha, tathA shrutirapyAhetyarthaH | tAM shrutimudAharati - aMsha iti | Adyo hiH prasiddhau | 'eShaH' jIvaH parasya 'aMshaH' tato nyUnatve sati tatsadR^ishatvarUpAMshatvavAniti pratij~nArthaH | dvitIyatR^itIyahishabdau bhedAbhedavyapadeshayorubhayorapi hetutvaj~nApakau | tathAchainaM jIvaM parasya sakAshAdyato bhinnamabhinnaM chAdhIyire shAkhinaH ata ityarthaH |
(8) samastasUtrArthe smR^itiM chAha - vArAhe cheti || na kevalaM sUtrakR^itaiva uktamidaM, kintu 'vArAhe' varAhapurANavachane.apyuktamityarthaH | putretyAdinA bahudhetyetadvivR^itam | yadvA putretyAdiH saMkShepaH bahudheti 
vistaraH | jIvasyeti sheShaH | tvapratyayasya pratyekaM sambandhaH | prakAre tR^itIyA | upalakShaNametat | asambandhitve chetyapi draShTavyam | 'gIyate' pratipAdyate 'tena' hetunA | tureva | jIvastasya hareraMsha eveti sambandhaH |
(9) evaM nAnAvyapadeshAdaMsho jIva ityuktvA yadanyathetyAdinoktaM bhedAbhedavyapadeshasyAMshatvAkShepakatvaM tadAha - yata iti || AdyashchaH prakArasamuchchaye, dvitIyo hetusamuchchaye tathA cha yato.ayaM jIvastasya haressakAshAt 'bhedena' bhinnatvenAbhedena cha prakAreNa 'gIyate' pratipAdyate ato.asya jIvasyAMshatvam 'uddiShTam' Abhiptamiti yojanA | nanu bhedAbhedavyapadeshAnyathA.anupapattyA bhedamaN^gIkR^itya abhedasthAne tannyUnatve sati tatsadR^ishatvarUpAMshatvaM kimarthamaN^gIkartavyam, mukhyato bhedAbhedAveva kiM na syAtAmityata Aha - bhedAbhedAviti | 'mukhyataH' sAkShAdvirodhAditi bhAvaH | itItyasya iti vArAha iti pUrveNAnvayaH tatashchAyaM chandrikArItyA sUtrArthaH - 'nAnAvyapadeshAt' pitR^itvaputratvAdinAnAprakAreNa jIvasya paramAtmopakartavyatvena tatsambandhitvokteH 'anyathA cha' 'na sambandhaH parasya, nAsAvasya' ityasambandhitvenApyuktaH jIvaH parasyAMsha ivAMshastadupajIvitvena tachCheShabhUtaH | kiJNcha - yataH 'eke' shAkhino 'anyathA' vakShyamANabhedApekShayA parAdbhedenainaM jIvam 'adhIyate' paThanti | evaM 'eke' pare shAkhinaH parabrahmaNaH 'dAshakitavAditvaM' dAshakitavadAsAdirUpajIvabhAvaM dAshakitavAderbrahmatvaM tadabhedamadhIyate, ato.api jIvaH parasya 'aMshaH' tannyUnatve sati tatsadR^ishatvarUpAMshatvopeta iti |
(10) evamupapattyA jIvasyeshvarAMshatvaM prasAdhya shrutyA.api tatsAdhayatsUtraM paThitvA tAM shrutimudAharati -mantreti| mantravarNaH shrutiH | chashabdo.atrAkarShaNIyaH| j~naH aMsha iti cha vartate| tathA cha na kevalamupapatteH, kintu 'pAdo.asya' iti mantravarNAchcha jIvaH parasyAMsha iti yojanA | 'vishvA bhUtAni' sarve jIvAH 'asya' paramAtmanaH 'pAdaH' aMsha iti shrutyarthaH prAgevoktaH | 
(11) smR^ityApi jIvasya paramAtmAMshatvaM sAdhayatsUtraM paThitvA tAM smR^itimudAharati - apIti || na kevalaM jIvasya paramAtmAMshatvaM shrUyate, kintu 'smaryate' smR^ityApyuchyate, ato.api jIvaH parasyAMsha ityanvayaH | 'jIvaloke' jIvachCharIre sthitaH 'sanAtanaH' nityo 'jIvabhUtaH' jIvabhAvopetaH jIvAkhyo yo brahmAdichetanarAshiH saH 'mamAMsha eva' madupajIvya eva madadhInatve sati matsadR^isha eva vA, na tu abhinnAMsho.anaMshove
tyarthaH | kR^iShNavAkyametat | kutaH? yata Ishvara eva jIvasya viShayAnubhavArthaM manaShShaShThAni | bahuvrIhiH | 'prakR^itisthAni' mUlakAraNasthAni sharIrasthAni vA j~nAnendriyANi 'karShati' AkarShati ata ityarthaH| IshvarashchAhameveti bhAvaH| tatra cha vivekaH - Ishvaro jIvasya sharIrAvAptau mUlakAraNAdindriyANi karShati, tadutkramaNe tu sharIrAt, sthitau tu golakAdibhya iti prameyadIpokto j~nAtavyaH |
(12) nanu jIvasyeshAMshatvaM na yuktam, tathA sati aMshatvAvisheShAt jIvAnAM matsyAdisAmyApAtAt, anaMshatvashrutivirodhAchchetyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramavatArayati - anaMshatveti || 'naivAMshaH' ityAdishruterityarthaH | 'gatiM' viShayaM, matsyAdyasAmyaM chashabdArthaH | 'Aha' arthAtsAkShAchcheti bhAvaH | aMshatvashruteH tadvirodhashAntyarthamiti sheShaH | pUrvasUtrAdapishabdamanuvartya naivaM para iti sUtrAMshaM vyAchaShTe - aMshatve.apIti | jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM cha bhagavadaMshatvAvisheShe.apItyarthaH | para ityasyArtho - 'matsyAdirUpI paraH' paramAtmeti | evamityasyArthaH - evaMvidha iti | jIvena sarvathA samo na, kutaH? yataH 'evaMvidho na' jIvavadbhinnAMsho na, kintu evaMvidhaH svarUpAMsha ityanuvR^ittyA yojanA | kevalAMshatvaM tu sarvasAmye na prayojakamiti bhAvaH | 
(13) nanu jIveShu bheda eva matsyAdiShvabheda eveti vaiShamyamanupapannam, ubhayoraMshatve visheShAbhAvAdityAshaN^kottaratvena pravR^ittaM prakAshAdivadityaMshaM
abhinnAMshAstu matsyAdyAstejasaH kAlavahnivat |
jIva bhinnAMshakAstatra tejasaH pratibimbavat ||
iti tattvapradIpoktapramANAnusAreNa vivR^iNoti - yatheti || evakAro.apyarthaH | chashabdaH samuchchaye | 'ekaprakAratA' ubhayorbhinnAMshatvAbhinnAMshatvAkhyaikaprakAratA na, kintu pralayakAlInAgnerabhinnAMshatvaM, khadyotashabditakITavisheShasya bhinnAMshatvamiti bhinnaprakArataivetyarthaH | sautrAdishabdagR^ihItadR^iShTAntAntaraM vivR^iNoti - yathA jalAMshasyeti | jalAMshasyApItyarthaH | jalAMshatvAvisheShe.apIti yAvat | 'amR^itasamudrasya' shuddhodakasamudrasya | mUtrAdeshchetyanantaraM naikaprakAratetyanuShajyate | kintvamR^itasamudrasyAbhinnAMshatvaM mUtrAderbhinnAMshatvameveti bhAvaH | Adipadena kashmalodakaM gR^ihyate | AdipadagR^ihItadR^iShTAntAntaraM vivR^iNoti - yathA pR^ithivIti | atrApyarthakaivakAro.anuShajyate, naikaprakArateti cha | kintu merugireH pR^ithivyabhinnAMshatvaM viShThAshabditAshuddhAdestu bhinnAMshatvameveti bhAvaH | tatheti sheShaH | pUrveNAnvayaH |
(14) nanu kAlAgnikhadyotayoH tejolakShaNabhUtakAryatvAt mUtrAmR^itasamudrayorablakShaNabhUtakAryatvAt meruviShThayoshcha pR^ithivIlakShaNabhUtakAryatvAt kAryakAraNAnAM cha siddhAntirbhedAbhedAbhyupagamena bhedAbhedasAmyAt kathametanmatsyAdInAmabhinnAMshatve jIvAnAM cha bhinnAMshatve dR^iShThAntA bhaverannityata Aha - abhimAnIti || prakAshAdyabhimAnidevatApekShayetyarthaH | etat prakAshAdivaditi dR^iShTAntAbhidhAnaM eteShAM dR^iShTAntatvaM vA | tathA 
cha tejojalapR^ithivyabhimAninInAM sUryavaruNadharANAM kAlAgnyamR^itasamudramervabhimAninAM tadaMshAnAM cha krameNAnyonyamabhinnatvAt, khadyotamUtraviShThAdyabhimAninInAm apabhraShTAkhyadevatAnAM tu krameNa tejojalapR^ithivyabhimAnibhyo bhinnatvAt yuktaM dR^iShTAntatvamiti bhAvaH | anena sUtre prakAshAdishabda ubhayavidhatejoMshAdiparo.abhimAnidevatAparashcha | tathA cha prakAshAdivadityasya kAlAgnikhadyotAdiShu deja AdyaMsheShveva bhinnatvAbhinnatvavaiShamyavadityartha ityuktaM bhavati | anenaivAnaMshatvashruterabhinnAMshatvaniShedhaparatvena gatiruktA bhavati | ata evAMshatvashruteH tadvirodho.api parihR^itaH |
(15) nanu dR^iShTAntamAtrasyAnirNAyakatvAt tatra tathAtve.api jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM cha svarUpAMshatvamabhedashcha kiM na syAdityAshaN^kAM smR^itibhiH pariharatsUtramupanyasyati - smaranti cheti || na kevalaM dR^iShTAntamAtrAdetaduchyate, kintu yataH smR^itikartAro jIvasya bhinnAMshatvaM matsyAderabhinnAMshatvaM cha smarantyato.apItyarthaH | 
(16) sUtrakR^idabhipretAH smR^itIrudAharati - eta iti || bhAgavate prathamaskandhe -
jagR^ihe pauruShaM rUpaM bhagavAnmahadAdibhiH |
sambhUtaM ShoDashakalamAdau lokasisR^ikShayA ||
ityanena yo bhagavAn prAk jagatsaMhR^itya chitprakR^ityAtmake pralayodake shrIparyaN^ke prakR^itimayatamasA nigUDhaH sthitaH sa eva lokasR^iShTIchChayA Adau punaH sR^iShTikAle svagUhakaM tamaH pItvA pralaye sUkShmarUpeNa svodaraniviShTairmahadahaN^kArAdibhiH sahitamekAdashendriyapaJNchabhUtAkhyaShoDashakalAyuktaM prANAdiShoDashakalAnvitaM vA 'pauruShaM' paramapuruShAkhyaM rUpaM 'jagR^ihe' vyaktamakarot ityaNDasR^iShTeH pUrvaM paramapuruShAkhyaM rUpam abhidhAyAtha 'yasyAmbhasi shayAnasya' ityanena aNDasR^iShTyanantaraM mahadAditattvadevaissahANDAntaHpraviShTAttasmAdeva paramapuruShAchchaturmukhajanakapadmayuN^nAbhiyutasheShashAyipadmanAbhAkhyarUpasyAbhivyaktimabhidhAya 'yasyAvayavasaMsthAnaiH' ityanena antarikShAdilokajanakaparamapuruShAkhyavirADrUpaM chAbhidhAya 'yasyAMshAMshena sR^ijyante devatiryaN^narAdayaH' ityanena sarve paramapuruShAMshavibhAgarUpatvenAvatiShThante tatsAmarthyaikadeshena jAyante chetyabhihite, ke te aMshA ityAkAN^kShAyAM 'dvitIyaM tu bhavAyAsya' ityArabhya 'athAsau yugasandhyAyAm' ityantena savistaraM varAhAdInAM bhagavadaMshatvamuktvA,
R^iShayo manavo devAH manuputrA mahaujasaH |
kalAH sarve harereva saprajApatayassmR^itAH ||
ityanena R^iShyAdInAM priyavratAdimanuputrANAM dakShAdiprajeshvarANAM cha jIvAnAmapi kalA ityanena bhagavadaMshatvamuktam | tatra kimavisheSheNa sarve aMshA ityAshaN^kAnirAsAya bhagavadavatAreShu jIva iva kalAtvasyopacharitatvashaN^kAvAraNAya cha 'ete' ityanena varAhAdInAM svarUpAMshatvamabhidhIyate | 'ete' varAhAdyA avatArAH 'puMsaH' paramapuruShasya nArAyaNasya 'svAMshakalAH' kalpyanta iti kalAH svarUpAMsharUpA eva vibhAgAH, na tu bhinnAMshAH, upachAreNa kalA iva kalA vA | bhedavadbhedAbhedAvapi netyAha - kR^iShNa ityAdinA | kR^iShNashabdo.ayaM 'kR^iShNo muktairijyate vItamohaiH' ityAdAviva nArAyaNe.asti| tushabdo.avadhAraNe| tathA cha ete na svAMshakalA ityetAvanmAtraM, kintu 'svayaM' sAkShAt bhagavAn kR^iShNo mUlarUpyeva tadatyantAbhinno.api| uktaM hi prameyadIpe -ete varAhAdyAH puMsaH svAMshakalAH| koà¤¼.arthaH? kR^iShNaH paramapuruSho bhagavAn svayameva eta iti svAMshakalA ityasyaiva bhedAbhedashaN^kAvAraNAyArthakathanaM, kR^iShNa ityAdItyasyAbhiprAyaH| AdisR^iShTAvavatIrNAH ete varAhAdaya eva indrAribhiH daittyairvyAkulaM pIDitaM janaM 'yugeyuge' punaravatIrya 'mR^iDayanti' rakShanti sukhayanti chetyarthaH | yathoktaM gItAbhAShye - 'rUpANyanekAnyasR^ijat prAdurbhAvabhavAya saH' iti | saH nArAyaNaH 'asR^ijat' vyabhajat | uttaratreti sheShaH |
(17) evaM varAhAdInAM svarUpAMshatvamuktvA R^iShaya ityAdinA bhagavadaMshatvenoktAnAM jIvAnAM bhinnAMshatvamuchyate - ataH paramityAdinA || yat 'ataH' paramapuruShAt jaDAchcha 'paraM' bhinnam 'avyaktam' akAryaM sUkShmamiti vA 'avyUDhaguNabR^iMhitam' anAdikAlAtkadAchidapi anapagatasattvAdiguNayuktaM chaitanyaM yachcha 'adR^iShTAshrutavastutvAt' shrutapadaM mananAderapyupalakShaNam | tathA cha ashrutAmatAnupAsitAsAkShAtkR^itaparamAtmasvarUpatvAt 'punarbhavaH' paunaHpunyena jAyamAno mriyamANashcha saMsArI sa jIva ityarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - adR^iShTAshrutavastutvAdityasya avyUDhaguNabR^iMhitamityanena anvaya uktaH | punarbhava ityanantaramiti bhAgavate iti sheShaH |
(18) na kevalamasaMsAritvasaMsAritvAbhyAM rakShakatvarakShyatvAbhyAM guNabandhAguNabandhAbhyAM matsyAdInAM jIvAnAM chAMshino.abhedabhedAvasAmyaM cha, kintu matsyAdInAM svarUpAMshalakShaNayuktatvAt jIvAnAM tu bhinnAMshalakShaNayogitvAt aMshinA bhedAbhedAvasAmyaM cheti bhAvena svarUpAsvarUpAMshavibhAgapUrvakaM tayorlakShaNaM tAvat smR^ityA darshayati - svAMshashcheti || svarUpAMsha ityarthaH | chashabdo dvedhaivetyavadhAraNArthaH | atho ityarthAntare | 'sAmarthyaM' jagatsR^iShTyAdilakShaNaM, tushchArthaH | 'yatsvarUpaM' yathA j~nAnAnandAdi 'yathA sthitiH' yathA sarvottamatvAdi | sudhArItyA sarvagatatvAdiparimANaM vA, deshataH kAlato guNataH vyAptatvena sthitiriti vA | tadeva 
svarUpAMshasya bhavatIti sheShaH | na tu tato bhinnamityevArthaH kuta ityata Aha - na bhedassvAMshAMshinoriti | svarUpAMshAMshinoH 'kvachidapi' kAle bhedo nAstItyarthaH | nanu kevalabhedAbhAve.api abhedasahitaH kiM na syAdityata Aha - aNumAtro.apIti | abhedasahito.apItyarthaH | vibhinnAMshalakShaNamAha - vibhinnAMsha iti | kiJNchitsAdR^ishyamAtrayugityetat sudhArItyA parameshvareNa chittvAdirUpeNa kiJNchitsAdR^ishyamAtrayugiti, aMshishabdamukhyavAchyena matsyAdinA kiJNchitsAdR^ishyaM tatsattayaiva sattAvattvarUpaM tanmAtrayugiti cha dvedhA vyAkhyeyam | mAtrashabdena sarvathA sAdR^ishyamabhedo bhedAbhedau cha nirastau |
(19) etachcha svarUpAMshatvalakShaNaM kR^iShNAdyavatAre.astIti smR^ityA.a.aha - neti || tvatsamo.anyo nAsti kuto.adhika ityarthaH | kR^iShNaM prati pArthavachanametat | gItAyAmiti sheShaH | saptamyantAnAM smarantItyanenAnvayaH | jIveShu bhinnAMshalakShaNavattvaM sAkShyanubhavasiddhamiti na tatra pramANamudAhR^itam | anena - yataH smR^itikAro matsyAdInAM jIvAnAM cha bhagavadaMshatvaM svarUpAsvarUpAMshatve tallakShaNe matsyAdInAM tadyogitvaM cha 'smaranti' bhAgavatAdismR^itiShu pratipAdayanti ato.api nobhayeShAm avisheSha iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(20) evaM jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM cha aMshinA krameNa bhedAbhedasadbhAvAnnaikavidhatetyuktam | yuktyantareNa cha ekavidhatAM parAkurvatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - anuj~neti || parAnuj~nayA pravR^ittirityanena sUtre parapadAnvayaH, jIvasya pravR^ittaye parAnuj~neti tattvapradIpokteH | anuj~nApadam anuj~nAsAdhyapravR^ittiparamiti sUchitam | parato bandhanivR^ittirityanena atrApi parapadAnvayaH, bandhasya yogyatayA sambandhaH, anuj~nA cha parihArashcheti vigrahashcha sUchitaH | jIvasya pravR^ittimokShayorubhayorapIshvarAdhInatvaj~nApanAyobhayatra parashabdaprayogaH | kechittu - parito hAraH parihAraH sarvakarmaNi jIvasya pravR^ittiH, bandhanivR^ittishcha parihAraH, parihArashcha parihArashcha parihArau, anuj~nayA parihArau anuj~nAparihArAviti tR^itIyAtatpuruSha iti parAnuj~nayetyAdibhAShyAnuj~nAsUtrAMshayorartha ityAhuH | chassamuchchaye | sUtre j~nasyetyanuvR^ittapadasyArtho jIvasyeti | vimatajIvasyetyarthaH | samudAyaikavachanamidam | anuvR^ittasyAperarthamAha - aMshatve.apIti | jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM chAMshatvAvisheShe.apItyarthaH | pratIyata ityasya pratyekamanvayaH | yata iti sheShaH | asyAto.api naivaM naikavidhatetyanuvR^ittasAdyenAnvayaH | pratIyate chetyapyanvayena sUtrachashabdAnuvR^ittissUchitA | kena hetunA pratIyata ityataH tatra dehasambandhAdityetadyojayati - deheti | svAMshikarmAnirmitadehasambandhitvAdityarthaH | svAMshipadaM paramAtmarUpabhinnAMshisvarUpAMshyubha
yaparam | tena nArjunAdau vyabhichAraH, na vA pakShe vimatajIve.aprasiddhiriti dhyeyam |
(21) na kevalaM dehasambandhAjjAvasyAnuj~nAparihArau pratIyete, kintu shrutyA.apItyAshayena tatra krameNa shrutI Aha - ya ityAdinA || 'yaH' iti shrutiH kartradhikaraNe 'tam' iti shrutishcha jij~nAsAdhikaraNe vyAkhyAtA | ityAdinetyasya pratIyata ityanenAnvayaH | chashabdo.atrAdhyAhAryaH | matsyAdInAmapi pravR^ittimokShayorIshvarAdhInatvAt kathaM naikavidhateyyata Aha - neti | parAnuj~nAparihArau netyarthaH | turvisheShe | 'parasya' matsyAdeH |
(22) netyetatkutaH ityato dehAsambandhAdeveti siddhe.apyatra shrutiM chAha - vAsudeva iti|| viShNuvAkyametat | ahaM vAsudevAdichaturmUrtiH, ahaM matsyAdidashamUrtiH 'rAmo' bhArgavaH, punashcha 'rAmo' dAsharathiH, kalkishabda ikArAnto.apyasti | ahaM 'shatadhA' nArAyaNAdishatarUpI aShTottaranAmavAchyasya nArAyaNAdeH alpatvAdaShTAvivakShayA shatadhetyuktiH | uktaM hi tattvapradIpe - shatadhA nAmAShTashatavAchyatvena shatarchina itivat sAmIpyAdavirodha iti | ahaM 'sahasradhA' vishvAdisahasranAmavAchyatvena sahasrarUpI | 'sahasradhA' sahasranAmavAchyatveneti tattvapradIpokteH | aham 'amitaH' parAdibahurUpI 'ahamanantaH' ajitAdyanantarUpItyarthaH | taduktaM bR^ihadAraNyakabhAShye - 
shataM nArAyaNAdyAtmA vishvAdyAtmA sahasrakam |
parAdirUpo bahudhA so.anantAtmA.ajitAdikaH || iti |
'ete' vAsudevAdyAH | 'eShAM' vAsudevAdInAm 'anuj~nA' pravR^ittyarthaM parAnuj~nA parAnuj~nayA pravR^ittiH 'muktiH' bandhAt | atra niShedhavAkyapaJNchakena jIvaniShThAnAM jananAdInAM bhagavadavatAreShu pratyekaM niShedhAt matsyAdInAmanekadhA jIvavaiShamyamupapAditam | anena sUtre anuj~nAparihArashabdau jananAdInAmapi upalakShakAvityuktaM bhavati | niShedhapaJNchake.api hetumAha - ete sarve pUrNA iti | 'amR^itAH' nityamaktAH | hishabdo hetau | vidhipaJNchakenApi matsyAdiShu IshvarasvarUpAMshalakShaNoktyA atathAbhUtAnAM matsyAdivaiShamyamupapAditaM bhavati | chaturvedashikhAyAmityanantaraM vachanAditi sheShaH | asya na tu parasya parato.anuj~nAparihArau sta iti pUrvavAkyenAnvayaH |
(23) yaduktaM jIvaH aMshiparamAtmAdhInapravR^ittyAdimAn svAMshikarmAnirmitadehasambandhitvAditi, tanna 
yujyate vyAptyabhAvAdityataH pravR^ittaM dR^iShTAntAMshaM sasheShaM yojayati - yujyate cheti || etaditi sheShaH | anena sUtre yujyate chetadityadhyAhArassUchitaH | 'etat' sAdhanam | sUtre jyotirAdivadityuktyA matsyAdiH svAMshyadhInapravR^ittirna bhavati svAMshikarmAnirmitadehAsambandhitvAt viyadgataprakAshAdyabhimAnivaditi yat prayogAntaramapyabhipretaM, tadapi yujyata ityAshayena dR^iShTAntavachanameva sphuTayati - yatheti | 'viyadgataH' antarikShagataH 'AdityaH' tanmaNDalAbhimAnI sUryaH aMshI tatprakAshaH | sUryaprakAshAbhimAnI sUryAMshashcha 'ekaprakAraH' ekavidhaH dvAvekalakShaNopetau, ata evAMshaH aMshyadhInAnuj~nAdirahita ityarthaH | tathA paro matsyAdishchaikaprakAra iti vAkyasheShaH |
(24) evaM jyotirAdivadityaMshaM dehasambandhitvahetorvyatirekavyAptau tadasambandhitvahetoranvayavyAptau dR^iShTAntaparatayA vyAkhyAya vaiparItyena tadubhayavyAptidR^iShTAntaparatayA.api vyAchaShTe - shuklamiti || yathetyatrApi saMyojyam | itItyanantaraM shrutAviti sheShaH | tadaMshasyApIti sUryamaNDalAMshatvenoktasyApItyarthaH | yadvA - maNDalAbhimAnyaMshatvena uktasyApItyarthaH | evamakShipadamapi chakShustadabhimAnyapabhraShTAkhyadevatobhayaparatayA vyAkhyeyam | yadyapitathApItyarthe.apishabdaH | ayaM bhAvaH - ChAndogye 'atha yadetadAdityasya shuklaM bhAH saiva R^ik, atha yannIlaM paraH kR^iShNaM tatsAma ..... atha yadetadakShNashshuklaM bhAH saiva R^ik, atha yannIlaM paraH kR^iShNam' (ChAM.1-6.7.) ityadhidaivatAdhyAtmaprakaraNagatavAkyadvayenAkShyAdityamaNDalayorubhayorapi shuklAdirUpatrayavattvoktyA sAmyaM siddham | evaM cha chakShuShi shrutyantarasiddhashuklAdirUpatrayavattvarUpAdityamaNDalasAmyasya 'trivR^idiva vai chakShuH shuklaM kR^iShNam' (ai.A.2.1.5.) ityaitareye kathitatvAt | tata eva tayoraMshAMshitve siddhe tadabhimAninorapi tatsidhyatyeveti | tattvapradIpe tu - bhAShye 'shuklaM kR^iShNaM kanInikA' iti na shrutigrahaNam, kintu svavachanenAkShyAdityayoH sAmyapradarshanameva | sAmyapradarshakashrutyanantaraM tUdAhartavyamityabhipretya 'shuklaM kR^iShNaM kanInikA' ityAdityasAdR^ishyAttadaMshatvamakShNaH 'atha yadetadAdityasya shuklaM bhAH saiva R^ik' ityAdishruterityuktam | aitareyashrutAvivashabdaH evArthaH| tritvena vartata iti trivR^it| tathA cha chakShushshuklakR^iShNakanInikAkR^iShNatArAvabhAsipuruSharUpeNa trivR^ideva vA ityarthaH| shrutyantaramapi R^iksAmashabditArdhanArInarAtmakavANIvAyuparatayA vyAkhyeyam| paraH kR^iShNamityetattu kanInikA paraH kR^iShNa iti tattvapradIpe vyAkhyAtam| na tAdR^ishIti | prabhAbhimAninoryAdR^ishI na tAdR^ishItyarthaH| apabhraShTAkhyadevatAnAM paradehasambandhaprayuktaparadehagatadoShaiH duShTatvAditi bhAvaH| tAsAM devatAtvaM tu antardhAnashaktyeti sudhAyAmuktam | na kevalaM chakShurdevasya tAdR^ishashaktyabhAvamAtraM, kintu tenAMshinA anugrAhyatvam | tenaivAvR^iterAvaraNasya viShayAvR^itibhUtasya tamaso 
nivR^ittishcha bhavatItyarthaH | tathA jIvAnAmapi dehasambandhAt matsyAdivachChaktyabhAva IshvarAnugrAhyatvaM, tata eva bandhanivR^ittishcha bhavet | na tu matsyAdInAM tadasambandhitvAditi vAkyasheShaH | anena sUtre jyotishshabdaH sUryatadabhinnabhinnAMshapara ityuktaM bhavati |
(25) sautrAdishabdagR^ihItaM dR^iShTAntaM vivR^iNoti - yathA bAhyeti || aNDAdbAhyashuddhajalAbhimAnivaruNasyAMshina ityarthaH | gR^ihAvaraNAdbAhyakUpAdijalAbhimAnino bhinnatvAttadvyAvR^ittyarthamamR^iteti | bahirAvaraNAdbAhyakUpAdijalAbhimAnino bhinnatvAttadvyAvR^ittyarthamamR^iteti | barihAvaraNodakasya bahutvAtsamudratvam, 'amR^itasamudrasya' saptamasamudrAbhimAnino varuNAMshasyetyarthaH | 'ekatvam' ekavidhatvamekashaktyupetatvamiti yAvat | lavaNAdisamudrAbhimAninAM bhinnAMshAnAmapi sattvAt tadvyAvR^ittyarthamatrApyamR^itetyuktam | evaM dehasambandhitvAsambandhitvahetorAdishabdagR^ihItavyatirekAnvayadR^iShTAntAvuktvA tayoreva tachChabdagR^ihItAnvayavyatirekadR^iShTAntAvAha - tadaMshasyeti| amR^itajalAbhimAnivaruNAMshasyetyarthaH | yathetyAdau yojyam | apishabdArthaH pUrvavat | 'shleShmaNaH' tadabhimAnyapabhraShTadevatAyAH ityarthaH | tachChabdadvayena varuNo gR^ihyate | virodhIti | 'shleShmA pittasya virodhI pittaM shleShmaNaH' iti shleShmavirodhinaH pittadhAtoH nivR^ittirbhavatItyarthaH | atra pUrvatra cha tatheti dArShTAntikavAkyAdhyAhAra uktarItyA kartavyaH |
(26) nanu yaduktaM jIvasya svAMshikarmAnirmitadehasambandhitvAdapabhraShTavadIshAdhInA pravR^ittiH, tato bandhanivR^ittishcheti | yachcha yathetyAdinA dR^iShTAntavivaraNena abhisaMhitaM dehAsambandhitvAdviyadgataprabhAbhimAnivat matsyAderIshvarAdhInapravR^ittyabhAva iti | taddvayamapyanupapannam | Adye matsyAdau vyabhichArAt, dvitIye dR^iShTAntAsiddherityata Aha - mokShadharme cheti || chashabdaH shaN^kAvyAvartakaH | yudhiShThiraM prati bhIShmavachanametat | he 'vishAM' prajAnAm ete asmin 'loke' jagati yatkiJNchijjIvajAtaM dehabaddhaM vartate, tadIshvarabuddhijaiH tannimittakaiH paJNchabhirbhUtaiH 'AviShTaM' baddhamityarthaH | evaM jIvAnAM bhautikadehasambandhamuktvA Ishvarasya tadasambandha uchyate - Ishvaro hIti | hirhetau, prasiddhau vA | hetUnevAha - mahaditi | mahachcha tadbhUtaM cha mahadbhUtaM bhUtebhyo 
mahaditi vA 'mahat' pUjyam aparichChinnaM 'bhUtaM' sadA sthitaM nirvikAraM vA | 'Ishvaro hi jagatsraShTA' iti gItAbhAShye paThitam | sa cheshvaro nAnyaH, kintu 'nArAyaNaH' muktAshrayo viShNuH visheSheNa rAjata iti 'virAT' nityAbhivyaktarUpaH | 'bhUtAntarAtmA' sarvajIvAntaryAmI 'varado' mokShadaH | vij~neya iti kvachitpAThaH | 'saguNaH' aishvaryAdiguNopetaH 'nirguNaH' sattvAdiguNAkAryadehaH | apichau samuchchaye | punarjIvasvarUpamuchyate - bhUteti | tasyeti sheShaH | asya tamiti yAvat | nR^ipashchAsAvatishayitasajjanashcha, tasya sambuddhiH nR^ipasattameti | he nR^ipasattama bhUtasambandhAdhInapralayopetamakAryatvAdavyaktashabditaM jIvachaitanyaM tasya nArAyaNasya shushrUShuH jij~nAsurbhavatIti jIvakartR^ikashushrUShAM prati prakR^ito nArAyaNaH karmatvena sambadhyata iti chandrikAkAraH | prameyadIpikAyAM tu - bhUtapralayasthAnabhUtA shrIH tasya prakR^itasya nArAyaNasya 'shushrUShuH' jij~nAsurbhavatIti jIvakartR^ikashushrUShAM prati prakR^ito nArAyaNaH karmatvena sambadhyata iti chandrikAkAraH | prameyadIpikAyAM tu - bhUtapralayasthAnabhUtA shrIH 'tasya' prakR^itasya nArAyaNasya shushrUShuH 'ye chApyakSharamavyaktam' iti smR^iteriti tattvapradIpAnusArAt kR^iShNasya mAnuShatanutvaM kuto netyavatArya sharIrANi hi bhautikAni bhavanti | bhUtAni cheshvarabuddhijAni tatkathaM tAni sambadhnIyuH | bhUtAni pralIyante yasmin tadvyaktaM tadabhimAnidevatA tasya shushrUShuH liN^gavyatyayaH ChAndasa iti vyAkhyAtam | tatra chandrikoktaH TIkAbhiprAyaH svarasaH | Ishvarasya jIvavailakShaNyapratipAdanArthaM pravR^itte mokShadharmavachane tasyaiva pratipAdanIyatayA lakShmIvailakShaNyapratipAdanasyehAsaN^gatatvAt | tattvapradIpaprameyadIpoktaM tvihAnabhipretamapi yojanAntaramityabhipretyoktaM chandrikAyAM tattvapradIpe yojanAntaramuktamiti | itItyasya iti mokShadharma ityanvayaH | ukteH na vyabhichArAsiddhaI iti vAkyasheShaH | tathA cha mokShadharme jIvAnAM bhautikadehasambandhasyoktatvAdAdyahetoH bhautikatvavisheShaNena matsyAdau vyabhichAro nirastaH | dvitIyasya svAMshikarmAnirmitatvavisheShaNAt dR^iShTAnte asiddhiH parihR^iteti bhAvaH| dvitIyahetau cha pakShe bhautikatvavisheShitadehasambandhitvarUpavisheShyAbhAvena dR^iShTAnte svAMsikarmAnirmitatvarUpavisheShaNAbhAvena vishiShTAbhAvarUpahetusattvopapAdanAya naJNdvayaprayoga iti dhyeyam | na cha 'Ishvaro hi' ityAdinAMshino nArAyaNasyaiva nirguNAdipadaiH dehAsambandhaH uktaH, nAMshAnAM matsyAdInAmiti kathaM tatra hetusiddhiriti vAchyam | 'yattaddadR^ishivAn brahmarUpaM hayashirodharam' iti hayagrIvAvatAraprasaN^ga evAsyoktatvenAsyAvatAraviShayatvAt | nArAyaNashabdastu aMshAnAM tadabhedAbhiprAya iti na tadanupapattiH |
(27) sUtrArthe smR^itiM chAha - vArAhe cheti || na kevalaM shrutisUtrAbhyAmukto.ayamarthaH, kintu vArAhe 
cheti chashabdArthaH | jIvAH aMshA apIti chashabdArthaH | dehayogyatvAdityanena muktA api AdyAnumAne pakShatvena saN^gR^ihItAH | anena dehasambandhayogyatvAdityarthaH | anumAnadvaye vyutkrameNa dR^iShTAntamAha - yatheti | sUryaprabhA chAkShi cheti vigrahaH | naikaprakAre iti sheShaH | 'amR^itasamudrasya' shuddhodakasamudrasya 'dvirUpatA' bhinnaprakAratA | 'anyasya' akShishleShmAdeH bhinnAMshasya 'tenaiva' aMshinaiva AvR^ittiH tamaHpittAdiH | tasya rodhanaM nivR^ittirbhavatItyarthaH | iti vArAhe ityanvayaH sUtroktamuktamiti sheShaH |
(28) yuktyantareNa matsyAdInAM jIvAnAM chaikavidhyaM parAkurvatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - asantateshcheti || apUrNashaktitvAdityanenAsantaterityasya samyaktatiH santatiH pUrNatAshaktyeti yogyatayA.anvaye naJNsambandhe chApUrNashaktitvAdityartha uktaH| sUtre bhAShye chashabdo na kevalamaMshyadhInapravR^ittitadabhAvAdinA jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM cha naikavidhatA, kintvasantateshcheti yuktisamuchchaye | anuvR^ittapadasyArthamAha - jIvasyeti | 'na matsyAdisAmyam' sarvasAmyamiti | anenAvyatikara ityasya naivaM para ityuktasya vyatyAsAbhAva iti vA, jIvAnAM matsyAdInAM cha shAstroktasvarUpasyAvyatyAsa iti vArtha ukto bhavati |
(29) matsyAdInAM pUrNashaktitvaM, na jIvasyetyetatkuta ityata Aha - tathA cheti || parAvarabhedena chetanadvaividhyamabhidhAya tatra paro nArAyaNa ityapyabhidhAya tasya vyUharUpANyuchyante - tasyetyAdinA | 'tasya' prasiddhasya 'etasya' prakR^itasya 'paramasya' nArAyaNasya kR^iShNo rAmaH kapila iti trINi rUpANItyanvayaH | tasyetyAdeH sarvatrAnvayagrahaNAya dvirgrahaNam | kR^iShNAditrayaM kashchana vyUhaH | na tu 'paJNchAtmakaH' ityuktasaptavyUhAntargatam | kechittu - kR^iShNAdikastu na vyUhaH nAtiriktavyUha iti TIkArthamAshritya saptavyUhAntargatamevaitadityAhuH | 'paJNcha' nArAyaNAdyaniruddhAntAni 'dasha' matsyAdIni shataM nArAyaNAdyaShTottarashatanAmavAchyAni | vishvAdIni sahasrANi | ajitAdInyanantAni rUpANi pUrNAni deshakAlAbhyAmanantAni guNataH asammitAni nirupamAni | atheti pratij~nAntaram | 'avarAH' chetanAH | uchyanta iti sheShaH | teShAM guNAnAha - sarva iti | 'apUrNAH' deshakAlaguNaiH badhyante paJNchabhirbhUtaiH | atha muchyante tebhya eva | apUrNatvabandhayoH sarvajIvasAdhAraNyAddviH sarvashabdaprayogaH | baddheShu sarvamuktau saMsArAbhAvApattyA kechanetyuktam | na cha krameNa sarvamuktau saMsArAbhAvaprasaN^ga ityAshaN^kAparihArAya sarve jIvAH anantA iti vipariNAmenAtrApi saMyojyam | saN^khyAto.anantA ityarthaH | apUrNAH badhyante atha muchyanta ityanena jIvAnAmapUrNatvabaddhatvAnityatvamuktatvAni IshvarAniShThAni sAmAnyAnyuktAni bhavanti | iti chaturvedashikhAyAmityanvayaH | yata uktamato na hetvasiddhiriti sheShaH |
(30) yuktyantareNoktamarthaM sAdhayatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - AbhAsa eveti || 'rUpaM rUpam' iti shrutyudAharaNenAbhAsatvahetorasiddhiH parihR^itA | pratibimbatvAditi | pratibimbAMshakatvAdityarthaH | anena AbhAsapadArtho.abhihitaH| yata iti sheShashcha sUchitaH | AbhAsapadasya tadadhInasattApratItikatvarUpapratibimbatvopetArthakatvaM cha bhA cha sA cha bhAse A sarvakAlavartinyau bhAse AbhAse, asya parashabdenAnvaye paramAtmAdhIne AbhAse pratItisatte yasyAsau parAbhAsa iti sudhoktarItyeti draShTavyam | chashabdaH pUrvoktahetusamuchchaye | evaM sUtre.api | evashabdastu anAbhAsatvavyAvartakaH, avyabhichArasUchakashcha | sUtre naivamityanuvR^ittasAdhyAMshasyArthamAha - na sAmyamiti | aMshatvAvisheShe.api na matsyAdisAmyamityarthaH | jIvasyetyanuvartate 
sAmyamekavidhatvam |
rUpaM rUpaM pratirUpo babhUva tadasya rUpaM pratichakShaNAya |
indro mAyAbhiH pururUpa Iyate yuktA hyasya harayaH shatA dasha || (R^i.6.47.18.)
iti R^iN^mantrasyAyamarthaH - 'shrR^iNve vIraH' (R^i.6.47.16.) ityAdinA prakR^itaH trividhajIvasamudAyaH asya parameshvarasya rUpaMrUpaM prati 'pratirUpaH' pratibimbo 'babhUva' pratibimbo bhUtvA vartate | tadbimbarUpamasya pratibimbatvenoktasya yogyajIvasya muktyarthaM 'pratichakShaNAya' sAkShAtkArAya bhavati tadviShayo bhavati | sa cha 'indraH' parameshvaraH 'mAyAbhiH' svasAmarthyaiH ichChAbhirvA pururUpaH anantajIvabimbarUpaH 'Iyate' j~nAyate | 'asya' Ishvarasya 'shatamanantaM bhavati' iti vachanAt shatAni ajitAdyanantarUpANi, evaM dashashatAni vishvAdisahasrarUpANi, evaM shatAni 'nArAyaNo naraH shauriH' ityAdIni, dasha matsyAdIni, evaM dasha bahUni parAdIni, 'harayo' harinAmakAni rUpANi 'yuktAH' vyUhashaH santi 'hi' prasiddhamiti |
(31) sUtrArthe smR^itiM chAha - vArAhe cheti || aMsha evAMshaka iti svArthe kapratyayaH | evamuttaratrApi | 'pare' svarUpAMshAH 'prAdurbhAvAH' matsyAdyavatArA ityarthaH | nanu jIvAnAM pratibimbAMshatvaM matsyAdInAM tu svarUpAMshatvamiti kutaH?, ubhayoH svarUpAMshatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha - pratibimbeShviti | yata iti sheShaH | sarvasAmye svarUpatvameva syAdato.alpetyuktam | 'svarUpANi' svarUpAMsharUpANi prAdurbhAvAtmakAni matsyAdIni itarANi alpasAmyavadbhinnAni yAvatsAmyavantItyarthaH | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | iti vArAha ityanvayaH | sUtrArtha ukta iti sheShaH |
(32) nanu na jIvasya paramAtmapratibimbAMshatvaM yuktam, jIvasvarUpAtiriktapratibimbopAdhyabhAvAdityata Aha - sopAdhiriti || iti shabdo.adhyAhAryaH | 'Iyate' j~nAyate | 'indrachApaH' tatsaMj~nakA vR^iShTisUchakadhanurAkR^itiH 'raveH' sUryasya tattejaso yathA nirupAdhipratibimbaH bimbAtiriktopAdAnopAdhyabhAvAt, ata eva na tasya sUryAtyantasAdR^ishyam, tathA jIvaH parasya hareH 'anupAdhiH' svarUpAtiriktopAdhirahitapratibimba ityarthaH | atra dR^iShTAnte bimbAtiriktopAdhyabhAvaH | dArShTAntike tu pratibimbAtiriktopAdhyabhAvaH | atiriktopAdhyabhAvastu ubhayatra sama iti draShTavyam | sopAdhipratibimbasya darpaNAdipratibimbitatvaM prasiddhameveti nodAhR^itam | kechittu - sopAdhipratibimbasya indrachApa udAharaNaM, tasya cha meghamaNDalaM vA sUryatejo vopAdhiH | upAdAnaM cha tadeva | nirupAdhipratibimbasya tu jIva udAharaNamiti yathAshabdAvR^ittyA vAkyadvayamapi dR^iShTAntaparatayA yojayanti | tattu chandrikAnanuguNatvAnmUlAbhAvAchchopekShyam | anena sUtrapaJNchakena jIvasya matsyAdivatsvarUpAMshatvAbhAvoktyA.anaMshatvashruteH svarUpAMshatvAbhAvaviShayatvena gatiruktA bhavati | shrutirityasya jIvasya pratibimbatvamuktvA.atiriktopAdhyabhAvamapi vaktIti sheShaH | ato nAtiriktopAdhyabhAve.api pratibimbatvahAniriti bhAvaH |
(33) jIvasya nirupAdhipratibimbatve ChAyArUpadR^iShTAntAntarapratipAdakaM ShaTprashnavAkyaM paThati - yatheti || yathA puruShasya dehasya ChAyA 'puruShe' dehe 'AtatA' tadadhInA tatpratirUpA bhavatIti yAvat | tadvat 'etasmin' puruShottame viShNau 'etat' pratibimbarUpaM vishvaM jIvajAtaM vA 'Atatam' AyattaM tadadhInatayA 
vartate tatpratibimbabhUtamityarthaH tattvapradIpokto dhyeyaH | atra sarvasyApi sharIrasya ChAyayA grastatvAt upahitAnupahitAMshadvayAbhAvAchChAyAyA indrachApavannirupAdhipratibimbatvoktiH | ChAyopAdAnaM tu nIrUpi dravyAntaramiti chandrikAkArAH | iti cheti | iti shrutishchoktArthamAhetyarthaH | chassamuchchaye |
|| iti aMshAdhikaraNam || 18 ||
|| 19. adR^iShTAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jIvasyeshvarapratibimbaviShayashrutivirodhaH parihriyate| viruddhashrutidvasyeha bhAShye anupanyAse.apyavyavahitasUtrabhAShye 'rUpaM rUpam' ityasyodAhR^itatvAt saikA vyavahitAtItasUtrabhAShye udAhR^itA 'naivAMsho na sambandhaH' (bhAllaveya.) itishrutiranyA saMshayabIjabhUteti draShTavyam | dvitIyashrutau sphuTamapratibimbatvasyApratipAdanAt TIkAyAmanumitatvoktiH| na jIvAH bhagavatpratibimbAH tathA shruteH, na jIvA ekapratibimbAH anyonyaM bhedavattvAddarpaNAdipratibimbataghaTapaTavadityanumAnAchcha| ataH sayuktikAnumitashrutivirodhAtpratibimbatvashrutirapramANamiti noktasamanvayasiddhirityevaM prApte siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - pratibimbAnAmiti| pratibimbatvenoktAnAM jIvAnAM tadabhyupagamya teShAM 'mithaH' parasparaM 'vaichitrye' suranaratiryagAdirUpabhede 'kAraNaM' kAraNAntaraM bimbavaichitryAdanyat| yadvA - apratibimbatvApekShayA.anyat| athavA IshashaktyapekShayA kAraNAntaraM adR^iShTAdivaichitryamAha sUtrakAra ityarthaH| vidyAkarmetyuktyA adR^iShTashabdo vidyopalakShakatayA vyAkhyAtaH| tena 'yathA praj~naM hi sambhavAH' ityAdishrutiH sUchitA| vaichitryAdityuktyA aniyamashabdo vyAkhyAtaH| punarvaichitryamityuktyA aniyamapadasyAvR^ittissUchitA| pUrvapUrvAdR^iShTavaichitryAduttarottarAdR^iShTavaichitryopapatteH nAdR^iShTavaichitryAsambhAvanAshaN^.hyetyAshayena - anAdItyuktam| upapadyate jIvAnAM yata iti sheShaH| anena yata ekeshvarAbhAsAnAmapi jIvAnAmadR^iShTAniyamAddevadAnavAdivaichitryamupapadyate, ato na tadanyathA.anupapattyA ekasya j~nasya pratibimbatvamupetyAnyeShAM tadabhAvo vAchyaH, kintu sarvo.api j~naH parAbhAsa iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | 
(2) devadAnavAdivaichitryasya rAgadveShamohAkhyadoShanimittakatvopapatteH kimadR^iShTakAraNakatvakalpanayetyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - abhisandhIti || na kevalaM suranarAdivaichitryaM, kintu ichChAdivaichitryaM cheti chashabdArthaH | 'ichChA' rAgaH | Adishabdena moho gR^ihyate | vaichitryamiti anuvR^ittAniyamapadavyAkhyAnam | evamityuktaM vyanakti - adR^iShTAditi | adR^iShTavaichitryAdityarthaH | bhavatIti sheShaH | na kAraNAntarAdityevArthaH | nanvasmAbhirapi siddhAntivatpUrvapUrvadoShavaichitryameva uttarottaradoShavaichitrye kAraNamityaN^gIkArAnna kvA.apyadR^iShTavaichitryApekShetyataH pravR^ittaM chashabdaM vyAchaShTe - chashabdeneti | pratikShaNeti | puruShavisheShaniShThapratikShaNavaichitryamityarthaH | saN^gR^ihItamiti sheShaH | chaH samuchchaye | anena - yato na kevalamAbhAse devadAnavAdAvaniyamo.adR^iShTaniyamAt, kintu abhisandhipadoktarAgAdiShvaniyamo.api tata eva bhavati, na rAgAdyaniyamAt | ato na tasmAtsurAsurAdivaichitryaM vAchyam | na kevalamabhisandhyAdiShu vaichitryamadR^iShTAniyamAt, kintvekapunniShThapratikShaNavaichitryaM cha 'evam' adR^iShTAniyamAdeva bhavati, na kAraNAntarAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | doShavaichitryAbhAve.api ekasmin puMsi pratikShaNavaichitryadarshanena kAraNAnveShaNe tatkAraNatayA.adR^iShTavaichitryasyaivAN^gIkAryatvAvashyakatvAt jIvavaichitrye.api tadeva kAraNamiti bhAvaH |
(3) nanu svargasthAH surAH, bhUmisthAH narAH, ityAdirUpeNa sthAnavaichitryAdeva suranarAdivaichitryopapatteH kimadR^iShTavaichitryeNetyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - pradeshAditi || atra pradeshapadaM tadvaichitryaparamityAha - svargeti | 'pradeshaH' sthAnaM 'vaichitryaM' suranarAdibhedaH | pratibimbAnAmiti vAchyamiti sheShaH | kuto na vAchyamityataH pravR^ittamantarbhAvAdityetattAtparyato vyAchaShTe - tatprApteriti | vichitrapradeshaprApterapyadR^iShTasApekShatvAdityarthaH | adR^iShTasyApekShA yasyAmiti vigrahaH | na kevalamAbhAsavaichitryasyetyapishabdArthaH | niShkAraNasthAnavaichitryasyaivAnupapattyA tatkAraNAnveShaNe antato.adR^iShTasyaiva tatkAraNatayA.aN^gIkAryatvAditi bhAvaH | anena pradeshavaichitryakAraNasyAdR^iShTa evAntarbhAvAttasyaitadrUpatvAditi sUtrakhaNDArtha ukto bhavati | yuktyantaramAha - eketi | ekasthAne sthitAnAmeva suranarAdijIvAnAmityarthaH | mitha iti sheShaH | tathA cha ito.apyadR^iShTavaichitryaM kAraNatayA.aN^gIkAryamiti bhAvaH | anenaikasthAnasthitAnAM mitho vaichitryakAraNasyAdR^iShTa evAntarbhAvAditi sUtrakhaNDasyArthAntaramuktaM bhavati | anena 'na sambandhaH' iti pratibimbvaniShedhakashruteH svarUpAtiriktopAdhinimittakapratibimbatvAbhAvaviShayatvAnna tadvirodho jIvapratibimbatvashruterityuktaM bhavati | 
|| iti adR^iShTAdhikaraNam || 19||
iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAchAryANAM sarvatantrasvatantrANAM 
shrImadraghunAthatIrthapUjyapAdAnAM shiShyeNa
shrImajjagannAthayatinA kR^itAyAM 
shrImadbrahmasUtrabhAShyadIpikAyAM
dvitIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH
|| OM ||
